}\r\n  if (c?.context_over_200k) {\r\n    result.experimentalOver200K = {\r\n      cache: {\r\n        read: c.context_over_200k.cache_read ?? 0,\r\n        write: c.context_over_200k.cache_write ??      for (const plugin of plugins) {\r\n          if (!plugin.auth) continue\r\n          const providerID = ProviderID.make(plugin.auth.provider)\r\n          if (disabled.has(providerID)) provider.env\r\n          if (provider.name) partial.name = provider.name\r\n          if (provider.options) partial.options = provider.options\r\n          mergeProvider(providerID, partial)\r\n        }\r\n\r\n        const gitlab = ProviderID.make(\"gitlab\")\r\n        if (discoveryLoaders[gitlab] && providers[gitlab] && isProviderAllowed(gitlab)) {\r\n          yield* Effect.promise(async () => {\r\n            try {\r\n              const discovered = await discoveryLoaders[gitlab]()\r\n              for (const [modelID, model] of Object.entries(discovered)) {\r\n                if log.warn(\"state discovery error\", { id: \"gitlab\", error: e })\r\n            }\r\n          })\r\n        }\r\n\r\n        for (const hook of plugins) {\r\n          const p = hook.provider\r\n          const models = p?.models\r\n          if (!p || !models) continue\r\n\r\n          const providerID = ProviderID.make(p.id)\r\n          if (disabled.has(providerID)) continue\r\n\r\n          const provider = providers[providerID]\r\n          if (!provider) continue\r\n          const pluginAuth = yield* auth.get(providerID).pipe(Effect.orDie)\r\n\r\n          provider.models = yield* ]),\r\n            )\r\n          })\r\n        }\r\n\r\n        for (const [id, provider] of Object.entries(providers)) {\r\n          const providerID = ProviderID.make(id)\r\n          if (!isProviderAllowed(providerID)) {\r\n            delete providers[providerID]\r\n            continue\r\n          }\r\n\r\n          const configProvider = cfg.provider?.[providerID]\r\n\r\n if (model.status === \"alpha\" && !Flag.OPENCODE_ENABLE_EXPERIMENTAL_MODELS) delete provider.models[modelID]\r\n            if (model.status === \"deprecated\") delete provider.models[modelID]\r\n            if (\r\n              (configProvider?.blacklist && configProvider.blacklist.includes(modelID)) ||\r\n              (configProvider?.whitelist &&          )\r\n            }\r\n          }\r\n\r\n          if (Object.keys(provider.models).length === 0) {\r\n            delete providers[providerID]\r\n            continue\r\n          }\r\n\r\n          log.info(\"found\", { providerID })\r\n        }\r\n\r\n        return {\r\n          models: languages,\r\n          providers,\r\n          sdk,\r\n          modelLoaders,\r\n          varsLoaders,\r\n        }\r\n      }),\r\n    )\r\n\r\n    const list = Effect.fn(\"Provider.list\")(() => InstanceState.use(state, (s) => s.providers))\r\n\r\n    async function resolveSDK(model: Model, s: State, envs: Record<string, string | undefined>) {\r\n      try {\r\n        using _ = log.time(\"getSDK\", {\r\n          providerID: model.providerID,\r\n        })\r\n        const provider = s.providers[model.providerID]\r\n        const options = { ...provider.options }\r\n\r\n        if (model.providerID === \"google-vertex\" && !model.api.npm.includes(\"@ai-sdk/openai-compatible\")) {\r\n          delete options.fetch\r\n        }\r\n\r\n        if (model.api.npm.includes(\"@ai-sdk/openai-compatible\") && options[\"includeUsage\"] !== false) {\r\n          options[\"includeUsage\"] = true\r\n        }\r\n\r\n        const baseURL = iife(() => {\r\n          let url =\r\n            typeof options[\"baseURL\"] === \"string\" && options[\"baseURL\"] !== \"\" ? options[\"baseURL\"] : model.api.url\r\n          if (!url) return\r\n\r\n          const loader = s.varsLoaders[model.providerID]\r\n          if (loader) {\r\n            const vars = loader(options)\r\n            for (const [key, value] of Object.entries(vars)) {\r\n              const field = \"${\" + key + \"}\"\r\n              url = url.replaceAll(field, value)\r\n            }\r\n          }\r\n\r\n          url = url.replace(/\\$\\{([^}]+)\\}/g, (item, key) => {\r\n            const val = envs[String(key)]\r\n            return val ?? item\r\n          })\r\n          return url\r\n        })\r\n\r\n        if (baseURL !== undefined) options[\"baseURL\"] = baseURL\r\n        if (options[\"apiKey\"] === undefined && provider.key) options[\"apiKey\"] = provider.key\r\n        if (model.headers)\r\n          options[\"headers\"] = {\r\n            ...options[\"headers\"],\r\n            ...model.headers,\r\n          }\r\n\r\n        const key = Hash.fast(\r\n          JSON.stringify({\r\n            providerID: model.providerID,\r\n            npm: model.api.npm,\r\n            options,\r\n          }),\r\n        )\r\n        const existing = s.sdk.get(key)\r\n        if (existing) return existing\r\n\r\n        const customFetch = options[\"fetch\"]\r\n        const chunkTimeout = options[\"chunkTimeout\"]\r\n        delete options[\"chunkTimeout\"]\r\n\r\n        options[\"fetch\"] = async (input: any, init?: BunFetchRequestInit) => {\r\n          const fetchFn = customFetch ?? fetch\r\n          const opts = init ?? {}\r\n          const chunkAbortCtl = typeof chunkTimeout === \"number\" && chunkTimeout > 0 ? new AbortController() : undefined\r\n          const signals: AbortSignal[] = []\r\n\r\n          if (opts.signal) signals.push(opts.signal)\r\n          if (chunkAbortCtl) signals.push(chunkAbortCtl.signal)\r\n          if (options[\"timeout\"] !== undefined && options[\"timeout\"] !== null && options[\"timeout\"] !== false)\r\n            signals.push(AbortSignal.timeout(options[\"timeout\"]))\r\n\r\n          const combined = signals.length === 0 ? null : signals.length === 1 ? signals[0] : AbortSignal.any(signals)\r\n          if (combined) opts.signal = combined\r\n\r\n          // Strip openai itemId metadata following what codex does\r\n          if (model.api.npm === \"@ai-sdk/openai\" && opts.body && opts.method === \"POST\") {\r\n            const body = JSON.parse(opts.body as string)\r\n            const isAzure = model.providerID.includes(\"azure\")\r\n            const keepIds = isAzure && body.store === true\r\n            if (!keepIds && Array.isArray(body.input)) {\r\n              for (const 		"content": "import { APICallError } from \"ai\"\r\nimport { STATUS_CODES } from \"http\"\r\nimport { iife } from \"@/util/iife\"\r\nimport type { ProviderID } from \"./schema\"\r\n\r\n// Adapted from overflow detection patterns in:\r\n// https://github.com/badlogic/pi-mono/blob/main/packages/ai/src/utils/overflow.ts\r\nconst OVERFLOW_PATTERNS = [\r\n  /prompt is too long/i, // Anthropic\r\n  /input is too long for requested model/i, // Amazon Bedrock\r\n  /exceeds the context window/i, // OpenAI (Completions + Responses API message text)\r\n  /input token count.*exceeds the maximum/i, // Google (Gemini)\r\n  /maximum prompt length is \\d+/i, // xAI (Grok)\r\n  /reduce the length of the messages/i, // Groq\r\n  /maximum context length is \\d+ tokens/i, // OpenRouter, DeepSeek, vLLM\r\n  /exceeds the limit of \\d+/i, // GitHub Copilot\r\n  /exceeds the available context size/i, // llama.cpp server\r\n  /greater than the context length/i, // LM Studio\r\n  /context window exceeds limit/i, // MiniMax\r\n  /exceeded model token limit/i, // Kimi For Coding, Moonshot\r\n  /context[_ ]length[_ ]exceeded/i, // Generic fallback\r\n  /request entity too large/i, // HTTP 413\r\n  /context length is only \\d+ tokens/i, // vLLM\r\n  /input length.*exceeds.*context length/i, // vLLM\r\n  /prompt too long; exceeded (?:max )?context length/i, // Ollama explicit overflow error\r\n  /too large for model with \\d+ maximum context length/i, // Mistral\r\n  /model_context_window_exceeded/i, // z.ai non-standard finish_reason surfaced as error text\r\n]\r\n\r\nfunction isOpenAiErrorRetryable(e: APICallError) {\r\n  const status = e.statusCode\r\n  if (!status) return e.isRetryable\r\n  // openai sometimes returns 404 for models that are actually available\r\n  return status === 404 || e.isRetryable\r\n}\r\n\r\n// Providers not reliably handled in this function:\r\n// - You may not have permission to access this resource — check your account and provider settings.\"\r\n      }\r\n      return msg\r\n    }\r\n\r\n    return `${msg}: ${e.responseBody}`\r\n  }).trim()\r\n}\r\n\r\nfunction json(input: unknown) {\r\n  if (typeof input === \"string\") {\r\n    try {\r\n      const result = JSON.parse(input)\r\n      if (result && typeof result === \"object\") return result\r\n      return undefined\r\n    } catch {\r\n      return undefined\r\n    }\r\n  }\r\n  if (typeof input === \"object\" && input !== null) {\r\n    return input\r\n  }\r\n  return undefined\r\n}\r\n\r\nexport type ParsedStreamError =\r\n  | {\r\n      type: \"context_overflow\"\r\n      message: string\r\n      responseBody: string\r\n    }\r\n  | {\r\n      type: \"api_error\"\r\n      message: string\r\n      isRetryable: false\r\n      responseBody: string\r\n    }\r\n\r\nexport function parseStreamError(input: unknown): ParsedStreamError | undefined {\r\n  const body = json(input)\r\n  if (!body) return\r\n\r\n  const responseBody = JSON.stringify(body)\r\n  if (body.type !== \"error\") return\r\n\r\n  switch (body?.error?.code) {\r\n    case \"context_length_exceeded\":\r\n      return {\r\n        type: \"context_overflow\",\r\n        message: \"Input exceeds context window of this model\",\r\n        responseBody,\r\n      }\r\n    case \"insufficient_quota\":\r\n      return {\r\n        type: \"api_error\",\r\n        message: \"Quota exceeded.     }\r\n      if (msg.role === \"tool\" && Array.isArray(msg.content)) {\r\n        return {\r\n          ...msg,\r\n          content: msg.content.map((part) => {\r\n            if (part.type ===   })\r\n  }\r\n  if ([\"@ai-sdk/anthropic\", \"@ai-sdk/google-vertex/anthropic\"].includes(model.api.npm)) {\r\n    // Anthropic rejects assistant turns where tool_use blocks are followed by Consecutive\r\n    // assistant messages are later merged by the provider/SDK, so preserving the\r\n    // original [tool_use...] then [text] order still produces the invalid payload.\r\n    //\r\n    // The root cause appears to be somewhere upstream where the stream is originally\r\n    // processed.   cache_control: { type: \"ephemeral\" },\r\n    },\r\n    copilot: {\r\n      copilot_cache_control: { type: \"ephemeral\" },\r\n    },\r\n    alibaba: {\r\n      cacheControl: { type: \"ephemeral\" },\r\n    },\r\n  }\r\n\r\n  for (const msg of unique([...system, ...final])) {\r\n    const useMessageLevelOptions =\r\n      model.providerID === \"anthropic\" ||\r\n      model.providerID.includes(\"bedrock\") ||\r\n      model.api.npm === \"@ai-sdk/amazon-bedrock\"\r\n    const shouldUseContentOptions = !useMessageLevelOptions && Array.isArray(msg.content) && msg.content.length > 0\r\n\r\n    if (shouldUseContentOptions) {\r\n      const lastContent = msg.content[msg.content.length - 1]\r\n      if (\r\n        lastContent &&\r\n        typeof lastContent === \"object\" &&\r\n        lastContent.type !== \"tool-approval-request\" &&\r\n        lastContent.type !== \"tool-approval-response\"\r\n      ) {\r\n        lastContent.providerOptions = mergeDeep(lastContent.providerOptions ?? {}, providerOptions)\r\n        continue\r\n      }\r\n    }\r\n\r\n    msg.providerOptions = mergeDeep(msg.providerOptions ?? {}, providerOptions)\r\n  }\r\n\r\n  return msgs\r\n}\r\n\r\nfunction unsupportedParts(msgs: ModelMessage[], model: Provider.Model): ModelMessage[] {\r\n  return msgs.map((msg) => {\r\n    if (msg.role !== \"user\" || !Array.isArray(msg.content)) return msg\r\n\r\n    const filtered = msg.content.map((part) => {\r\n      if (part.type !== \"file\" && part.type !== \"image\") return part\r\n\r\n      // Check for empty base64 image data\r\n      if (part.type === \"image\") {\r\n        const imageStr = String(part.image)\r\n        if (imageStr.startsWith(\"data:\")) {\r\n          const match = imageStr.match(/^data:([^;]+);base64,(.*)$/)\r\n          if (match && (!match[2] || match[2].length === 0)) {\r\n            return {\r\n              type: \"text\" as const,\r\n              text: \"ERROR: Image file is empty or corrupted. Please provide a valid image.\",\r\n            }\r\n          }\r\n        }\r\n      }\r\n\r\n      const mime = part.type === \"image\" ? String(part.image).split(\";\")[0].replace(\"data:\", \"\") : part.mediaType\r\n      const filename = part.type === \"file\" ? part.filename : undefined\r\n      const modality = mimeToModality(mime)\r\n      if (!modality) return part\r\n      if (model.capabilities.input[modality]) return part\r\n\r\n      const name = filename ? `\"${filename}\"` : modality\r\n      return {\r\n        type: \"text\" as const,\r\n        text: `ERROR: Cannot read ${name} (this model does not support ${modality} input). Inform the user.`,\r\n      }\r\n    })\r\n\r\n    return { ...msg, content: filtered }\r\n  })\r\n}\r\n\r\nexport function message(msgs: ModelMessage[], model: Provider.Model, options: Record<string, unknown>) {\r\n  msgs = unsupportedParts(msgs, model)\r\n  msgs = normalizeMessages(msgs, model, options)\r\n  if (\r\n    (model.providerID === \"anthropic\" ||\r\n      model.providerID === \"google-vertex-anthropic\" ||\r\n      model.api.id.includes(\"anthropic\") ||\r\n      model.api.id.includes(\"claude\") ||\r\n      model.id.includes(\"anthropic\") ||\r\n      model.id.includes(\"claude\") ||\r\n      model.api.npm === \"@ai-sdk/anthropic\" ||\r\n      model.api.npm === \"@ai-sdk/alibaba\") &&\r\n    model.api.npm !== \"@ai-sdk/gateway\"\r\n  ) {\r\n    msgs = applyCaching(msgs, model)\r\n  }\r\n\r\n  // Remap providerOptions keys from stored providerID to expected SDK key\r\n  const key = sdkKey(model.api.npm)\r\n  if (key && key !== model.providerID) {\r\n    const remap = (opts: Record<string, any> | undefined) => {\r\n      if (!opts) return opts\r\n      if (!(model.providerID in opts)) return opts\r\n      const result = { ...opts }\r\n      result[key] = result[model.providerID]\r\n      delete result[model.providerID]\r\n      return result\r\n    }\r\n\r\n    msgs = msgs.map((msg) => {\r\n      if (!Array.isArray(msg.content)) return { ...msg, providerOptions: remap(msg.providerOptions) }\r\n      return {\r\n        ...msg,\r\n        providerOptions: remap(msg.providerOptions),\r\n        content: msg.content.map((part) => {\r\n          if (part.type === \"tool-approval-request\" || part.type === \"tool-approval-response\") {\r\n            return { ...part }\r\n          }\r\n          return { ...part, providerOptions: remap(part.providerOptions) }\r\n        }),\r\n      } as typeof msg\r\n    })\r\n  }\r\n\r\n  return msgs\r\n}\r\n\r\nexport function temperature(model: Provider.Model) {\r\n  const id = model.id.toLowerCase()\r\n  if (id.includes(\"qwen\")) return 0.55\r\n  if (id.includes(\"claude\")) return undefined\r\n  if (id.includes(\"gemini\")) return 1.0\r\n  if (id.includes(\"glm-4.6\")) return 1.0\r\n  if (id.includes(\"glm-4.7\")) return 1.0\r\n  if (id.includes(\"minimax-m2\")) return 1.0\r\n  if (id.includes(\"kimi-k2\")) {\r\n    // kimi-k2-thinking & kimi-k2.5 && kimi-k2p5 && kimi-k2-5\r\n    if ([\"thinking\", \"k2.\", \"k2p\", \"k2-5\"].some((s) => id.includes(s))) {\r\n      return 1.0\r\n    }\r\n    return 0.6\r\n  }\r\n  return undefined\r\n}\r\n\r\nexport function topP(model: Provider.Model) {\r\n  const id = model.id.toLowerCase()\r\n  if (id.includes(\"qwen\")) return 1\r\n  if ([\"minimax-m2\", \"gemini\", \"kimi-k2.5\", \"kimi-k2p5\", \"kimi-k2-5\"].some((s) => id.includes(s))) {\r\n    return 0.95\r\n  }\r\n  return undefined\r\n}\r\n\r\nexport function topK(model: Provider.Model) {\r\n  const id = model.id.toLowerCase()\r\n  if (id.includes(\"minimax-m2\")) {\r\n    if ([\"m2.\", \"m25\", \"m21\"].some((s) => id.includes(s))) return 40\r\n    return 20\r\n  }\r\n  if (id.includes(\"gemini\")) return 64\r\n  return undefined\r\n}\r\n\r\nconst WIDELY_SUPPORTED_EFFORTS = [\"low\", \"medium\", \"high\"]\r\nconst OPENAI_EFFORTS = [\"none\", \"minimal\", ...WIDELY_SUPPORTED_EFFORTS, \"xhigh\"]\r\n\r\nfunction anthropicAdaptiveEfforts(apiId: string): string[] | null {\r\n  if ([\"opus-4-7\", \"opus-4.7\"].some((v) => apiId.includes(v))) {\r\n    return [\"low\", \"medium\", \"high\", \"xhigh\", \"max\"]\r\n  }\r\n  if ([\"opus-4-6\", \"opus-4.6\", \"sonnet-4-6\", \"sonnet-4.6\"].some((v) => apiId.includes(v))) {\r\n    return [\"low\", \"medium\", \"high\", \"max\"]\r\n  }\r\n  return null\r\n}\r\n\r\nexport function variants(model: Provider.Model): Record<string, Record<string, any>> {\r\n  if (!model.capabilities.reasoning) return {}\r\n\r\n  const id = model.id.toLowerCase()\r\n  const adaptiveEfforts = anthropicAdaptiveEfforts(model.api.id)\r\n  if (\r\n    id.includes(\"deepseek\") ||\r\n    id.includes(\"minimax\") ||\r\n    id.includes(\"glm\") ||\r\n    id.includes(\"kimi\") ||\r\n    id.includes(\"k2p\") ||\r\n    id.includes(\"qwen\") ||\r\n    id.includes(\"big-pickle\")\r\n  )\r\n    return {}\r\n\r\n  // see: https://docs.x.ai/docs/guides/reasoning#control-how-hard-the-model-thinks\r\n  if (id.includes(\"grok\") && id.includes(\"grok-3-mini\")) {\r\n    if (model.api.npm === \"@openrouter/ai-sdk-provider\") {\r\n      return {\r\n        low: { reasoning: { effort: \"low\" } },\r\n        high: { reasoning: { effort: \"high\" } },\r\n      }\r\n    }\r\n    return {\r\n      low: { reasoningEffort: \"low\" },\r\n      high: { reasoningEffort: \"high\" },\r\n    }\r\n  }\r\n  if (id.includes(\"grok\")) return {}\r\n\r\n  switch (model.api.npm) {\r\n    case \"@openrouter/ai-sdk-provider\":\r\n      if (!model.id.includes(\"gpt\") && !model.id.includes(\"gemini-3\") && !model.id.includes(\"claude\")) return {}\r\n      return (adaptiveEfforts) {\r\n          return Object.fromEntries(\r\n            adaptiveEfforts.map((effort) => [\r\n              effort,\r\n              {\r\n                thinking: {\r\n                  type: \"adaptive\",\r\n                },\r\n                effort,\r\n              },\r\n            ]),\r\n          )\r\n        }\r\n        return {\r\n          high: {\r\n \"enabled\",\r\n              budgetTokens: 31999,\r\n            },\r\n          },\r\n        }\r\n      }\r\n      if (model.id.includes(\"google\")) {\r\n        if (id.includes(\"2.5\")) {\r\n          return {\r\n            high: {\r\n              thinkingConfig: {\r\n                includeThoughts: true,\r\n                thinkingBudget: 16000,\r\n              },\r\n            },\r\n            max: {\r\n              thinkingConfig: {\r\n                includeThoughts: true,\r\n                thinkingBudget: 24576,\r\n              },\r\n            },\r\n          }\r\n        }\r\n        return Object.fromEntries(\r\n          [\"low\", \"high\"].map((effort) => [\r\n            effort,\r\n            {\r\n              includeThoughts: true,\r\n              thinkingLevel: effort,\r\n            },\r\n          ]),\r\n        )\r\n      }\r\n      return Object.fromEntries(OPENAI_EFFORTS.map((effort) => [effort, { reasoningEffort: effort }]))\r\n\r\n    case \"@ai-sdk/github-copilot\":\r\n      if (model.id.includes(\"gemini\")) {\r\n        // currently github copilot only returns thinking\r\n        return {}\r\n      }\r\n      if (model.id.includes(\"claude\")) {\r\n        return Object.fromEntries(WIDELY_SUPPORTED_EFFORTS.map((effort) => [effort, { reasoningEffort: effort }]))\r\n      }\r\n      const copilotEfforts = iife(() => {\r\n        if (id.includes(\"5.1-codex-max\") || id.includes(\"5.2\") || id.includes(\"5.3\"))\r\n          return [...WIDELY_SUPPORTED_EFFORTS, \"xhigh\"]\r\n        const arr = case \"@ai-sdk/togetherai\":\r\n    // https://v5.ai-sdk.dev/providers/ai-sdk-providers/togetherai\r\n    case \"@ai-sdk/xai\":\r\n    // https://v5.ai-sdk.dev/providers/ai-sdk-providers/xai\r\n    case \"@ai-sdk/deepinfra\":\r\n    // https://v5.ai-sdk.dev/providers/ai-sdk-providers/deepinfra\r\n    case \"venice-ai-sdk-provider\":\r\n    // https://docs.venice.ai/overview/guides/reasoning-models#reasoning-effort\r\n    case \"@ai-sdk/openai-compatible\":\r\n      return Object.fromEntries(WIDELY_SUPPORTED_EFFORTS.map((effort) => [effort, { reasoningEffort: effort }]))\r\n\r\n    case \"@ai-sdk/azure\":\r\n      // https://v5.ai-sdk.dev/providers/ai-sdk-providers/azure\r\n      if (id === \"o1-mini\") return {}\r\n      const azureEfforts = [\"low\", \"medium\", \"high\"]\r\n      if (id.includes(\"gpt-5-\") || id === \"gpt-5\") {\r\n        azureEfforts.unshift(\"minimal\")\r\n      }\r\n      return include: [\"reasoning.encrypted_content\"],\r\n          },\r\n        ]),\r\n      )\r\n    case \"@ai-sdk/openai\":\r\n      // https://v5.ai-sdk.dev/providers/ai-sdk-providers/openai\r\n      if (id === \"gpt-5-pro\") return {}\r\n      const openaiEfforts = iife(() => {\r\n        if (id.includes(\"codex\")) {\r\n          if (id.includes(\"5.2\") || id.includes(\"5.3\")) return [...WIDELY_SUPPORTED_EFFORTS, \"xhigh\"]\r\n          return WIDELY_SUPPORTED_EFFORTS\r\n        }\r\n        const arr = [...WIDELY_SUPPORTED_EFFORTS]\r\n        if (id.includes(\"gpt-5-\") || id === \"gpt-5\") {\r\n          arr.unshift(\"minimal\")\r\n        }\r\n        if (model.release_date >= \"2025-11-13\") {\r\n          arr.unshift(\"none\")\r\n        }\r\n        if (model.release_date >= \"2025-12-04\") {\r\n          arr.push(\"xhigh\")\r\n        }\r\n        return arr\r\n      })\r\n      return Object.fromEntries(\r\n        openaiEfforts.map((effort) => [\r\n          effort,\r\n          {\r\n            reasoningEffort: effort,\r\n            reasoningSummary: \"auto\",\r\n            include: [\"reasoning.encrypted_content\"],\r\n          },\r\n        ]),\r\n      )\r\n\r\n    case \"@ai-sdk/anthropic\":\r\n    // https://v5.ai-sdk.dev/providers/ai-sdk-providers/anthropic\r\n    case \"@ai-sdk/google-vertex/anthropic\":\r\n      // https://v5.ai-sdk.dev/providers/ai-sdk-providers/google-vertex#anthropic-provider\r\n\r\n      if (model.providerID === \"github-copilot\") {\r\n        if (model.api.id.includes(\"opus-4.7\")) {\r\n          return Object.fromEntries([\"medium\"].map((effort) => [effort, { reasoningEffort: effort }]))\r\n        }\r\n      }\r\n\r\n      if (adaptiveEfforts) {\r\n        return ...(model.api.id.includes(\"opus-4-7\") || model.api.id.includes(\"opus-4.7\")\r\n                  ? { display: \"summarized\" }\r\n                  : {}),\r\n              },\r\n              effort,\r\n            },\r\n          ]),\r\n        )\r\n      }\r\n\r\n      return {\r\n        high: {\r\n          thinking: {\r\n            type: \"enabled\",\r\n            budgetTokens: Math.min(16_000, Math.floor(model.limit.output / 2 - 1)),\r\n          },\r\n        },\r\n        max: {\r\n          thinking: {\r\n            type: \"enabled\",\r\n            budgetTokens: Math.min(31_999, model.limit.output - 1),\r\n          },\r\n        },\r\n      }\r\n\r\n    case \"@ai-sdk/amazon-bedrock\":\r\n      // https://v5.ai-sdk.dev/providers/ai-sdk-providers/amazon-bedrock\r\n      if (adaptiveEfforts) {\r\n        return Object.fromEntries(\r\n          adaptiveEfforts.map((effort) => [\r\n            effort,\r\n            {\r\n              reasoningConfig: {\r\n                type: \"adaptive\",\r\n                maxReasoningEffort: effort,\r\n                ...(model.api.id.includes(\"opus-4-7\") || model.api.id.includes(\"opus-4.7\")\r\n                  ? { display: \"summarized\" }\r\n                  : {}),\r\n              },\r\n            },\r\n          ]),\r\n        )\r\n      }\r\n      // For Anthropic models on Bedrock, use reasoningConfig with budgetTokens\r\n      if (model.api.id.includes(\"anthropic\")) {\r\n        return {\r\n          high: {\r\n            reasoningConfig: {\r\n              type: \"enabled\",\r\n              budgetTokens: 16000,\r\n            },\r\n          },\r\n          max: {\r\n            reasoningConfig: {\r\n              type: \"enabled\",\r\n              budgetTokens: 31999,\r\n            },\r\n          },\r\n        }\r\n      }\r\n\r\n      // For Amazon Nova models, use reasoningConfig with maxReasoningEffort\r\n      return Object.fromEntries(\r\n        WIDELY_SUPPORTED_EFFORTS.map((effort) => [\r\n          effort,\r\n          {\r\n            reasoningConfig: {\r\n              type: \"enabled\",\r\n              maxReasoningEffort: effort,\r\n            },\r\n          },\r\n        ]),\r\n      )\r\n\r\n    case \"@ai-sdk/google-vertex\":\r\n    // https://v5.ai-sdk.dev/providers/ai-sdk-providers/google-vertex\r\n    case \"@ai-sdk/google\":\r\n      // https://v5.ai-sdk.dev/providers/ai-sdk-providers/google-generative-ai\r\n      if (id.includes(\"2.5\")) {\r\n        return {\r\n          high: {\r\n            thinkingConfig: {\r\n              includeThoughts: true,\r\n              thinkingBudget: 16000,\r\n            },\r\n          },\r\n          max: {\r\n            thinkingConfig: {\r\n              includeThoughts: true,\r\n              thinkingBudget: 24576,\r\n            },\r\n          },\r\n        }\r\n      }\r\n      let levels = [\"low\", \"high\"]\r\n      if (id.includes(\"3.1\")) {\r\n        levels = [\"low\", \"medium\", \"high\"]\r\n      }\r\n\r\n      return Object.fromEntries(\r\n        levels.map((effort) => [\r\n          effort,\r\n          {\r\n            thinkingConfig: {\r\n              includeThoughts: true,\r\n              thinkingLevel: effort,\r\n            },\r\n          },\r\n        ]),\r\n      )\r\n\r\n    case \"@ai-sdk/mistral\":\r\n      // https://v5.ai-sdk.dev/providers/ai-sdk-providers/mistral\r\n      // https://docs.mistral.ai/capabilities/reasoning/adjustable\r\n      if (!model.capabilities.reasoning) return {}\r\n      // Only Mistral Small 4 supports reasoning (mistral-small-2603,   case \"@ai-sdk/groq\":\r\n      // https://v5.ai-sdk.dev/providers/ai-sdk-providers/groq\r\n      const groqEffort = [\"none\", ...WIDELY_SUPPORTED_EFFORTS]\r\n      return Object.fromEntries(\r\n        groqEffort.map((effort) => [\r\n          effort,\r\n          {\r\n            reasoningEffort: effort,\r\n          },\r\n        ]),\r\n      )\r\n\r\n    case \"@ai-sdk/perplexity\":\r\n      // https://v5.ai-sdk.dev/providers/ai-sdk-providers/perplexity\r\n      return {}\r\n\r\n    case \"@jerome-benoit/sap-ai-provider-v2\":\r\n      if (model.api.id.includes(\"anthropic\")) {\r\n        type: \"adaptive\",\r\n                },\r\n                effort,\r\n              },\r\n            ]),\r\n          )\r\n        }\r\n        return {\r\n          high: {\r\n \"enabled\",\r\n              budgetTokens: 31999,\r\n            },\r\n          },\r\n        }\r\n      }\r\n      if (model.api.id.includes(\"gemini\") && id.includes(\"2.5\")) {\r\n        return     thinkingConfig: {\r\n              includeThoughts: true,\r\n              thinkingBudget: 24576,\r\n            },\r\n          },\r\n        }\r\n      }\r\n      if }\r\n      return {}\r\n  }\r\n  return {}\r\n}\r\n\r\nexport function options(input: {\r\n  model: Provider.Model\r\n  sessionID: string\r\n  providerOptions?: Record<string, any>\r\n}): Record<string, any> {\r\n  const result: Record<string, any> = {}\r\n\r\n  // openai and providers using openai package should set store to false by default.\r\n  if (\r\n    input.model.providerID === \"openai\" ||\r\n    input.model.api.npm === \"@ai-sdk/openai\" ||\r\n    input.model.api.npm === \"@ai-sdk/github-copilot\"\r\n  ) {\r\n    result[\"store\"] = false\r\n  }\r\n\r\n  if (input.model.api.npm === \"@ai-sdk/azure\") {\r\n    result[\"store\"] = true\r\n    result[\"promptCacheKey\"] = input.sessionID\r\n  }\r\n\r\n  if (input.model.api.npm === \"@openrouter/ai-sdk-provider\" || input.model.api.npm === \"@llmgateway/ai-sdk-provider\") {\r\n    result[\"usage\"] = {\r\n      include: true,\r\n    }\r\n    if (input.model.api.id.includes(\"gemini-3\")) {\r\n      result[\"reasoning\"] = { effort: \"high\" }\r\n    }\r\n  }\r\n\r\n  if (\r\n    input.model.providerID === \"baseten\" ||\r\n    (input.model.providerID === \"opencode\" && [\"kimi-k2-thinking\", \"glm-4.6\"].includes(input.model.api.id))\r\n  ) {\r\n    result[\"chat_template_args\"] = { enable_thinking: true }\r\n  }\r\n\r\n  if (\r\n    [\"zai\", \"zhipuai\"].some((id) => input.model.providerID.includes(id)) &&\r\n    input.model.api.npm === \"@ai-sdk/openai-compatible\"\r\n  ) {\r\n    result[\"thinking\"] = {\r\n      type: \"enabled\",\r\n      clear_thinking: false,\r\n    }\r\n  }\r\n\r\n  if (input.model.providerID === \"openai\" || input.providerOptions?.setCacheKey) {\r\n    result[\"promptCacheKey\"] = input.sessionID\r\n  }\r\n\r\n  if (input.model.api.npm === \"@ai-sdk/google\" || input.model.api.npm === \"@ai-sdk/google-vertex\") {\r\n    if (input.model.capabilities.reasoning) {\r\n      result[\"thinkingConfig\"] = {\r\n        includeThoughts: true,\r\n      }\r\n      if (input.model.api.id.includes(\"gemini-3\")) {\r\n        result[\"thinkingConfig\"][\"thinkingLevel\"] = \"high\"\r\n      }\r\n    }\r\n  }\r\n\r\n  // Enable thinking by default for kimi models using anthropic SDK\r\n  const modelId = input.model.api.id.toLowerCase()\r\n  if (\r\n    (input.model.api.npm === \"@ai-sdk/anthropic\" || input.model.api.npm === \"@ai-sdk/google-vertex/anthropic\") &&\r\n    (modelId.includes(\"k2p\") || modelId.includes(\"kimi-k2.\") || input.model.api.id.includes(\"gpt-5.\") &&\r\n      !input.model.api.id.includes(\"codex\") &&\r\n      !input.model.api.id.includes(\"-chat\") &&\r\n      input.model.providerID !== \"azure\"\r\n 		"content": "现在我已经完整阅读了所有相关的核心文件，下面是详细分析。\n\n---\n\n## opencode Provider 系统分析\n\n### 1. 整体架构概览\n\nProvider 系统是一个**分层加载、可插件扩展、基于 Effect 架构**的 AI 模型提供者管理系统。核心代码位于 `packages/opencode/src/provider/` 目录下：\n\n```\nprovider/\n├── index.ts          # 命名空间导出\n├── provider.ts       # 核心：Provider 服务层（加载、初始化、查询、获取 LanguageModel）\n├── schema.ts         # ProviderID / ModelID 的 branded types\n├── models.ts         # 从 models.dev 远程拉取/本地缓存的 provider & model 数据\n├── auth.ts           # Provider 认证（OAuth / API Key）\n├── error.ts          # API 调用错误的解析（上下文溢出、配额超限等）\n├── transform.ts      # 消息转换、推理变体、缓存注入等\n└── sdk/\n    └── copilot/      # GitHub Copilot 自定义 SDK（chat / responses）\n```\n\n### 2. 数据来源：三层模型发现\n\nProvider 系统从三个渠道获取 provider 和 model 信息，**层层覆盖**：\n\n#### 层 1: models.dev（远程 + 本地快照）\n- `models.ts` 中的 `Data` 是一个 lazy initializer\n- **加载顺序**：本地 cache 文件 → 构建时快照 `models-snapshot.js` → 远程 `https://models.dev/api.json`\n- 返回一个 `Record<string, Provider>`，每个 Provider 包含 `{ id, name, env, models[] }`\n- 后台每 60 分钟自动刷新\n\n#### 层 2: 配置文件（`opencode.json` 中的 `provider` 字段）\n- 用户可以通过配置文件自定义 provider\n- 可以**新增 provider**，也可以**覆盖已有的 models.dev provider**（覆盖 name、models、options 等）\n- 支持 `whitelist` / `blacklist` 筛选模型\n- 支持 `enabled_providers` / `disabled_providers` 全局开关\n\n#### 层 3: 环境变量 + 已存储的 API Key\n- 读取 `Env` 中的环境变量（每个 provider 的 `env` 字段定义了它监听的变量名）\n- 读取 `Auth` 中已存储的 API Key / OAuth token\n\n### 3. Provider 加载流程（`provider.ts` 中的 `layer`）\n\n核心初始化流程在 `layer`（一个 Effect Layer）中：\n\n```\n1. 读取 config     → 获取用户配置、enabled/disabled\n2. 加载 models.dev → 得到 database（基础模型数据）\n3. 加载 config providers → 覆盖/扩充 database\n4. 加载环境变量    → 检查 env 中是否有对应 provider 的 API key\n5. 加载 Auth API keys → 检查已存储的 auth 信息\n6. 加载插件 auth loader\n7. 执行 custom() 函数 → 为每个 provider 运行自定义初始化逻辑\n8. 重新应用 config → 确保用户配置覆盖生效\n9. 运行 discoverModels（如 GitLab 的动态模型发现）\n10. 运行插件 provider hooks\n11. 过滤：disabled、alpha/deprecated、whitelist/blacklist\n```\n\n关键函数 `custom(dep)` 为每个已知 provider 定义了**定制化初始化逻辑**，包括：\n- `autoload`: 是否自动加载（无需用户显式配置）\n- `getModel`: 自定义模型获取函数（如 `github-copilot` 判断用 `chat()` 还是 `responses()`）\n- `vars`: 环境变量映射（如 `google-vertex` 设置 `GOOGLE_VERTEX_PROJECT`）\n- `options`: 传递给 SDK 的默认选项（如 `anthropic` 注入 headers）\n- `discoverModels`: 动态模型发现（如 `gitlab` 从 GitLab API 获取 workflow models）\n\n### 4. 内置 Provider 列表\n\n系统通过 `BUNDLED_PROVIDERS`（静态导入映射）和 `custom()`（动态初始化逻辑）支持以下提供者：\n\n| npm 包 | 提供者 |\n|---|---|\n| `@ai-sdk/amazon-bedrock` | Amazon Bedrock |\n| `@ai-sdk/anthropic` | Anthropic (Claude) |\n| `@ai-sdk/azure` | Azure OpenAI |\n| `@ai-sdk/google` | Google Gemini |\n| `@ai-sdk/google-vertex` | Google Vertex AI |\n| `@ai-sdk/google-vertex/anthropic` | Vertex Anthropic |\n| `@ai-sdk/openai` | OpenAI |\n| `@ai-sdk/openai-compatible` | 通用 OpenAI 兼容 |\n| `@openrouter/ai-sdk-provider` | OpenRouter |\n| `@ai-sdk/xai` | xAI (Grok) |\n| `@ai-sdk/mistral` | Mistral |\n| `@ai-sdk/groq` | Groq |\n| `@ai-sdk/deepinfra` | DeepInfra |\n| `@ai-sdk/deepseek` | DeepSeek |\n| `@ai-sdk/cerebras` | Cerebras |\n| `@ai-sdk/cohere` | Cohere |\n| `@ai-sdk/gateway` | AI Gateway |\n| `@ai-sdk/togetherai` | Together AI |\n| `@ai-sdk/perplexity` | Perplexity |\n| `@ai-sdk/vercel` | Vercel |\n| `@ai-sdk/alibaba` | Alibaba |\n| `@ai-sdk/github-copilot` | GitHub Copilot (自定义 SDK) |\n| `gitlab-ai-provider` | GitLab Duo |\n| `venice-ai-sdk-provider` | Venice.ai |\n\n另外还有 `opencode`（自有推断服务）、`sap-ai-core`、`cloudflare-workers-ai`、`cloudflare-ai-gateway`、`llmgateway`、`nvidia`、`kilo`、`zenmux` 等。\n\n### 5. SDK 解析与模型实例化\n\n`resolveSDK()` 函数负责将 `Model` 解析为 AI SDK 的 `LanguageModelV3`：\n\n1. 从 provider options 和 model api 信息拼接 `baseURL`\n2. 注入 API key、headers\n3. 设置自定义 `fetch`（含超时、SSE chunk timeout、OpenAI itemId 清理）\n4. 先查 `BUNDLED_PROVIDERS`（已内联的 npm 包，无需额外安装）\n5. 否则通过 `Npm.add(npm_package)` 按需安装\n6. 动态 `import` 并调用 `createXxx()` 工厂函数\n7. 结果缓存到 `sdk Map`（以 `providerID + npm + options` 的 hash 为 key）\n\n`getLanguage()` 进一步将 SDK 实例与 model 绑定：\n- 如果该 provider 有自定义 `modelLoaders`（如 `github-copilot` 的 `chat()` vs `responses()` 切换），走自定义路径\n- 否则调用 `sdk.languageModel(model.api.id)`\n- 结果也缓存（key = `${providerID}/${model.id}`）\n\n### 6. 认证系统（`auth.ts`）\n\n`ProviderAuth` 服务提供：\n- `methods()`: 返回每个 provider 的认证方法（OAuth / API Key + 交互式 prompts）\n- `authorize()`: 触发 OAuth 流程或 API Key 的验证\n- `callback()`: 处理 OAuth 回调，将 token 或 API key 存入 `Auth` 服务\n\n认证由**插件系统**驱动——插件可以声明 `auth` hook，定义认证方法和 UI 提示。\n\n### 7. 消息转换与推理变体（`transform.ts`）\n\n`transform.ts` 负责在调用模型前对消息进行各种**规范化处理**：\n\n- **`normalizeMessages()`**: 按 provider 清理消息格式（如 Anthropic 拒绝空内容、Mistral 的 toolCallId 清洗、DeepSeek 注入 reasoning_content）\n- **`unsupportedParts()`**: 检查模型是否支持用户发送的多模态内容，不支持则替换为错误文本\n- **`applyCaching()`**: 为支持缓存的 provider（Anthropic、Bedrock、OpenRouter 等）注入缓存控制标记\n- **`variants()`**: 为支持推理（reasoning）的模型生成变体配置（如 reasoningEffort 的高低级别）\n- **`options()` / `smallOptions()`**: 根据模型和 provider 生成默认的调用选项\n\n### 8. 配置结构（`config/provider.ts`）\n\n用户可在 `opencode.json` 中配置：\n\n```json\n{\n  \"provider\": {\n    \"anthropic\": {\n      \"api\": \"https://api.anthropic.com\",\n      \"name\": \"My Anthropic\",\n      \"env\": [\"ANTHROPIC_API_KEY\"],\n      \"options\": { \"baseURL\": \"...\" },\n      \"models\": {\n        \"claude-sonnet-4\": {\n          \"cost\": { \"input\": 3, \"output\": 15 },\n          \"limit\": { \"context\": 200000, \"output\": 8192 }\n        }\n      }\n    }\n  },\n  \"disabled_providers\": [\"some-provider\"],\n  \"enabled_providers\": [\"openai\", \"anthropic\"],\n  \"model\": \"anthropic/claude-sonnet-4\",\n  \"small_model\": \"anthropic/claude-haiku-4-5\"\n}\n```\n\n### 9. Service 接口\n\nProvider 服务暴露的核心接口：\n\n```typescript\ninterface Interface {\n  readonly list: () => Effect.Effect<Record<ProviderID, Info>>\n  readonly getProvider: (providerID: ProviderID) => Effect.Effect<Info>\n  readonly getModel: (providerID: ProviderID, modelID: ModelID) => Effect.Effect<Model>\n  readonly getLanguage: (model: Model) => Effect.Effect<LanguageModelV3>\n  readonly closest: (providerID: ProviderID, query: string[]) => Effect.Effect<...>\n  readonly getSmallModel: (providerID: ProviderID) => Effect.Effect<Model | undefined>\n  readonly defaultModel: () => Effect.Effect<{ providerID: ProviderID; modelID: ModelID }>\n}\n```\n\n### 10. 错误处理（`error.ts`）\n\n- `parseAPICallError()`: 将 AI SDK 的 `APICallError` 解析为 `context_overflow` 或 `api_error`\n- 支持大量 provider 的溢出错误模式匹配（Anthropic、OpenAI、Google、Bedrock、Groq 等）\n- 特殊处理 OpenAI 的 404 retryable 行为\n\n---\n\n### 总结\n\nopencode 的 Provider 系统是一个**高度可扩展的分层架构**：\n\n1. **数据层**：远程模型目录 → 配置文件 → 环境变量/Auth，逐层覆盖\n2. **加载层**：内置 bundled providers + 按需 npm 安装 + 自定义 SDK\n3. **定制层**：每个 provider 有独立的初始化逻辑（autoload、getModel、vars、options）\n4. **转换层**：消息规范化、缓存注入、推理变体、多模态过滤\n5. **插件层**：插件可以通过 `auth` 和 `provider` hooks 扩展认证方式和模型发现\n6. **认证层**：支持 OAuth 和 API Key 两种方式，由插件驱动交互流程",
		"reasoning": "现在我对 opencode 的 Provider 系统有了全面的了解。让我整理一下分析结果。",
		"role": "assistant",
		"tool_calls": []
	}
]
```

})\r\n\r\nfunction shouldUseCopilotResponsesApi(modelID: string): boolean {\r\n  const match = /^gpt-(\\d+)/.exec(modelID)\r\n  if (!match) return false\r\n  return Number(match[1]) >= 5 && !modelID.startsWith(\"gpt-5-mini\")\r\n}\r\n\r\nfunction wrapSSE(res: Response, ms: number, ctl: AbortController) {\r\n  if (typeof ms !== \"number\" || ms <= 0) return res\r\n  if (!res.body) return res\r\n  if (!res.headers.get(\"content-type\")?.includes(\"text/event-stream\")) return res\r\n\r\n  const reader = res.body.getReader()\r\n  const body = new ReadableStream<Uint8Array>({\r\n    async pull(ctrl) {\r\n      const part = await new Promise<Awaited<ReturnType<typeof reader.read>>>((resolve, reject) => {\r\n        const id = setTimeout(() => {\r\n          const err = new Error(\"SSE read timed out\")\r\n          ctl.abort(err)\r\n          void reader.cancel(err)\r\n          reject(err)\r\n        }, ms)\r\n\r\n        reader.read().then(\r\n          (part) => {\r\n            clearTimeout(id)\r\n            resolve(part)\r\n          },\r\n          (err) => {\r\n            clearTimeout(id)\r\n            reject(err)\r\n          },\r\n        )\r\n      })\r\n\r\n      if (part.done) {\r\n        ctrl.close()\r\n        return\r\n      }\r\n\r\n      ctrl.enqueue(part.value)\r\n    },\r\n    async cancel(reason) {\r\n      ctl.abort(reason)\r\n      await reader.cancel(reason)\r\n    },\r\n  })\r\n\r\n  return new Response(body, {\r\n    headers: new Headers(res.headers),\r\n    status: res.status,\r\n    statusText: res.statusText,\r\n  })\r\n}\r\n\r\ntype BundledSDK = {\r\n  languageModel(modelId: string): LanguageModelV3\r\n}\r\n\r\nconst BUNDLED_PROVIDERS: Record<string, () => Promise<(opts: any) => BundledSDK>> = {\r\n  \"@ai-sdk/amazon-bedrock\": () => import(\"@ai-sdk/amazon-bedrock\").then((m) => m.createAmazonBedrock),\r\n  \"@ai-sdk/anthropic\": () => import(\"@ai-sdk/anthropic\").then((m) => (!accountId)\r\n        return {\r\n          autoload: false,\r\n          async getModel() {\r\n            throw new Error(\r\n              \"CLOUDFLARE_ACCOUNT_ID is missing. Set it with: export CLOUDFLARE_ACCOUNT_ID=<your-account-id>\",\r\n            )\r\n          },\r\n        }\r\n\r\n      const apiKey = yield* Effect.gen(function* () {\r\n        const envToken = env[\"CLOUDFLARE_API_KEY\"]\r\n        if (envToken) return envToken\r\n        if (auth?.type === \"api\") return auth.key\r\n        return undefined\r\n      })\r\n\r\n      return {\r\n        autoload: !!apiKey,\r\n        options: {\r\n          apiKey,\r\n          headers: {\r\n            \"User-Agent\": `opencode/${InstallationVersion} cloudflare-workers-ai (${os.platform()} ${os.release()}; ${os.arch()})`,\r\n          },\r\n        },\r\n        async getModel(sdk: any, modelID: string) {\r\n          return sdk.languageModel(modelID)\r\n        },\r\n        vars(_options) {\r\n          return {\r\n            CLOUDFLARE_ACCOUNT_ID: accountId,\r\n          }\r\n        },\r\n      }\r\n    }),\r\n    \"cloudflare-ai-gateway\": Effect.fnUntraced(function* (input: Info) {\r\n      // When baseURL is already configured (e.g. corporate config), skip the ID checks.\r\n      if (input.options?.baseURL) return { autoload: false }\r\n\r\n      const auth = yield* dep.auth(input.id)\r\n      const env = yield* dep.env()\r\n      const accountId = env[\"CLOUDFLARE_ACCOUNT_ID\"] || (auth?.type === \"api\" ? auth.metadata?.accountId : undefined)\r\n      const gateway = env[\"CLOUDFLARE_GATEWAY_ID\"] || (auth?.type === \"api\" ? auth.metadata?.gatewayId : undefined)\r\n\r\n      if (!accountId || !gateway) {\r\n        const missing = [\r\n          !accountId ? \"CLOUDFLARE_ACCOUNT_ID\" : undefined,\r\n          !gateway ? \"CLOUDFLARE_GATEWAY_ID\" : undefined,\r\n        ].filter((x): x is string => Boolean(x))\r\n        return {\r\n          autoload: false,\r\n          async getModel() {\r\n            throw new Error(\r\n              `${missing.join(\" and \")} missing. Set with: ${missing.map((x) => `export ${x}=<value>`).join(\" && \")}`,\r\n            )\r\n          },\r\n        }\r\n      }\r\n\r\n      // Get API token from env or auth - required for (or CF_AIG_TOKEN) is required for Cloudflare AI Gateway. \" +\r\n            \"Set it via environment variable or run `opencode auth cloudflare-ai-gateway`.\",\r\n        )\r\n      }\r\n\r\n      // Use official ai-gateway-provider package (v2.x for AI SDK v5 compatibility)\r\n      const { createAiGateway } = yield* Effect.promise(() => import(\"ai-gateway-provider\"))\r\n      const { createUnified } = yield* Effect.promise(() => import(\"ai-gateway-provider/providers/unified\"))\r\n\r\n      const metadata = iife(() => {\r\n        if (input.options?.metadata) return input.options.metadata\r\n        try {\r\n          return JSON.parse(input.options?.headers?.[\"cf-aig-metadata\"])\r\n        } catch {\r\n          return undefined\r\n        }\r\n      })\r\n      const opts = {\r\n        metadata,\r\n        cacheTtl: input.options?.cacheTtl,\r\n        cacheKey: input.options?.cacheKey,\r\n        skipCache: input.options?.skipCache,\r\n        collectLog: input.options?.collectLog,\r\n        headers: {\r\n          \"User-Agent\": `opencode/${InstallationVersion} cloudflare-ai-gateway (${os.platform()} ${os.release()}; ${os.arch()})`,\r\n        },\r\n      }\r\n\r\n      const aigateway = createAiGateway({\r\n        accountId,\r\n        gateway,\r\n        apiKey: apiToken,\r\n        ...(Object.values(opts).some((v) => v !== undefined) ? { options: opts } : {}),\r\n      })\r\n      const unified = createUnified()\r\n\r\n      return {\r\n        autoload: true,\r\n        async getModel(_sdk: any, modelID: string, _options?: options: {},\r\n      }\r\n    }),\r\n    cerebras: () =>\r\n      Effect.succeed({\r\n        autoload: false,\r\n        options: {\r\n          headers: {\r\n            \"X-Cerebras-3rd-Party-Integration\": \"opencode\",\r\n          },\r\n        },\r\n      }),\r\n    kilo: () =>\r\n      Effect.succeed({\r\n        autoload: false,\r\n        options: {\r\n          headers: {\r\n            \"HTTP-Referer\": \"https://opencode.ai/\",\r\n            \"X-Title\": \"opencode\",\r\n          },\r\n        },\r\n      }),\r\n  }\r\n}\r\n\r\nconst ProviderApiInfo =   field: Schema.Literals([\"reasoning_content\", \"reasoning_details\"]),\r\n  }),\r\n])\r\n\r\nconst ProviderCapabilities = Schema.Struct({\r\n  temperature: Schema.Boolean,\r\n  reasoning: }\r\n  if (c?.context_over_200k) {\r\n    result.experimentalOver200K = {\r\n      cache: {\r\n        read: c.context_over_200k.cache_read ?? 0,\r\n        write: c.context_over_200k.cache_write ?? },\r\n              options: mergeDeep(existingModel?.options ?? {}, model.options ?? {}),\r\n              limit: {\r\n                context: model.limit?.context ?? existingModel?.limit?.context            source: \"api\",\r\n              key: provider.key,\r\n            })\r\n          }\r\n        }\r\n\r\n        // plugin auth loader - database now has entries for config providers\r\n        for (const plugin of plugins) {\r\n          if (!plugin.auth) continue\r\n          const providerID = ProviderID.make(plugin.auth.provider)\r\n          if (disabled.has(providerID)) 		"content": "import { APICallError } from \"ai\"\r\nimport { STATUS_CODES } from \"http\"\r\nimport { iife } from \"@/util/iife\"\r\nimport type { ProviderID } from \"./schema\"\r\n\r\n// Adapted from overflow detection patterns in:\r\n// https://github.com/badlogic/pi-mono/blob/main/packages/ai/src/utils/overflow.ts\r\nconst OVERFLOW_PATTERNS = [\r\n  /prompt is too long/i, // Anthropic\r\n  /input is too long for requested model/i, // Amazon Bedrock\r\n  /exceeds the context window/i, // OpenAI (Completions + Responses API message text)\r\n  /input token count.*exceeds the maximum/i, // Google (Gemini)\r\n  /maximum prompt length is \\d+/i, // xAI (Grok)\r\n  /reduce the length of the messages/i, // Groq\r\n  /maximum context length is \\d+ tokens/i, // OpenRouter, DeepSeek, vLLM\r\n  /exceeds the limit of \\d+/i, // GitHub Copilot\r\n  /exceeds the available context size/i, // llama.cpp server\r\n  /greater than the context length/i, // LM Studio\r\n  /context window exceeds limit/i, // MiniMax\r\n  /exceeded model token limit/i, // Kimi For Coding, Moonshot\r\n  /context[_ ]length[_ ]exceeded/i, // Generic fallback\r\n  /request entity too large/i, // HTTP 413\r\n  /context length is only \\d+ tokens/i, // vLLM\r\n  /input length.*exceeds.*context length/i, // vLLM\r\n  /prompt too long; exceeded (?:max )?context length/i, // Ollama explicit overflow error\r\n  /too large for model with \\d+ maximum context length/i, // Mistral\r\n  /model_context_window_exceeded/i, // z.ai non-standard finish_reason surfaced as error text\r\n]\r\n\r\nfunction isOpenAiErrorRetryable(e: APICallError) {\r\n  const status = e.statusCode\r\n  if (!status) return e.isRetryable\r\n  // openai sometimes returns 404 for models that are actually available\r\n  return status === 404 || e.isRetryable\r\n}\r\n\r\n// Providers not reliably handled in this function:\r\n// - z.ai: can accept overflow silently (needs token-count/context-window checks)\r\nfunction isOverflow(message: string) {\r\n  if (OVERFLOW_PATTERNS.some((p) => p.test(message))) return true\r\n\r\n  // Providers/status patterns handled outside of regex list:\r\n  // - Cerebras: often returns \"400 (no body)\" / \"413 (no body)\"\r\n  // - Mistral: often returns \"400 (no body)\" / \"413 (no body)\"\r\n  return /^4(00|13)\\s*(status code)?\\s*\\(no body\\)/i.test(message)\r\n}\r\n\r\nfunction message(providerID: ProviderID, e: APICallError) {\r\n  return iife(() => {\r\n    const msg = e.message\r\n    if (msg === \"\") {\r\n      if (e.responseBody) return e.responseBody\r\n      if (e.statusCode) {\r\n        const err = STATUS_CODES[e.statusCode]\r\n        if (err) return err\r\n      }\r\n      return \"Unknown error\"\r\n    }\r\n\r\n    if (!e.responseBody || (e.statusCode && msg !== STATUS_CODES[e.statusCode])) {\r\n      return msg\r\n    }\r\n\r\n    try {\r\n      const body = JSON.parse(e.responseBody)\r\n      // try to extract common error message fields\r\n      const errMsg = body.message || body.error || body.error?.message\r\n      if (errMsg && typeof errMsg === \"string\") {\r\n        return `${msg}: ${errMsg}`\r\n      }\r\n    } catch {}\r\n\r\n    // If responseBody is HTML (e.g. from a gateway or proxy error page),\r\n    // provide a human-readable message instead of dumping raw markup\r\n    if (/^\\s*<!doctype|^\\s*<html/i.test(e.responseBody)) {\r\n      if (e.statusCode === 401) {\r\n        return \"Unauthorized: request was blocked by a gateway or proxy. Your authentication token may be missing or expired — try running `opencode auth login <your provider URL>` to re-authenticate.\"\r\n      }\r\n      if (e.statusCode === 403) {\r\n        return \"Forbidden: request was blocked by a gateway or proxy. You may not have permission to access this resource — check your account and provider settings.\"\r\n      }\r\n      return msg\r\n    }\r\n\r\n    return `${msg}: ${e.responseBody}`\r\n  }).trim()\r\n}\r\n\r\nfunction json(input: unknown) {\r\n  if (typeof input === \"string\") {\r\n    try {\r\n      const result = JSON.parse(input)\r\n      if (result && typeof result === \"object\") return result\r\n      return undefined\r\n    } catch {\r\n      return undefined\r\n    }\r\n  }\r\n  if (typeof input === \"object\" && input !== null) {\r\n    return input\r\n  }\r\n  return undefined\r\n}\r\n\r\nexport type ParsedStreamError =\r\n  | {\r\n      type: \"context_overflow\"\r\n      message: string\r\n      responseBody: string\r\n    }\r\n  | {\r\n      type: \"api_error\"\r\n      message: string\r\n      isRetryable: false\r\n      responseBody: string\r\n    }\r\n\r\nexport function parseStreamError(input: unknown): ParsedStreamError | undefined {\r\n  const body = json(input)\r\n  if (!body) return\r\n\r\n  const responseBody = JSON.stringify(body)\r\n  if (body.type !== \"error\") return\r\n\r\n  switch (body?.error?.code) {\r\n    case \"context_length_exceeded\":\r\n      return {\r\n        type: \"context_overflow\",\r\n        message: \"Input exceeds context window of this model\",\r\n        responseBody,\r\n      }\r\n    case \"insufficient_quota\":\r\n      return {\r\n        type: \"api_error\",\r\n        message: \"Quota exceeded. model: Provider.Model,\r\n  _options: Record<string, unknown>,\r\n): ModelMessage[] {\r\n  // Anthropic rejects messages with empty content - filter out empty string messages\r\n  // and remove empty     }\r\n      if (msg.role === \"tool\" && Array.isArray(msg.content)) {\r\n        return {\r\n          ...msg,\r\n          content: msg.content.map((part) => {\r\n            if (part.type === \"tool-result\") {\r\n              return { ...part, toolCallId: scrub(part.toolCallId) }\r\n            }\r\n            return part\r\n          }),\r\n        }\r\n      }\r\n      return msg\r\n    })\r\n  }\r\n  if ([\"@ai-sdk/anthropic\", \"@ai-sdk/google-vertex/anthropic\"].includes(model.api.npm)) {\r\n    // Anthropic rejects assistant turns where tool_use blocks are followed by non-tool\r\n    // content, e.g. [tool_use, tool_use, text], with:\r\n    // `tool_use` ids were found without `tool_result` blocks immediately after...\r\n    //\r\n    // Reorder that invalid shape into [text] + [tool_use, tool_use]. Consecutive\r\n    // assistant messages are later merged by the provider/SDK, so preserving the\r\n    // original [tool_use...] then [text] order still produces the invalid payload.\r\n    //\r\n    // The root cause appears to be somewhere upstream where the stream is originally\r\n    // processed. We were unable to locate an exact narrower reproduction elsewhere,\r\n    // so we keep this transform in place for the time being.\r\n    msgs = msgs.flatMap((msg) => {\r\n      if (msg.role !== \"assistant\" || !Array.isArray(msg.content)) return [msg]\r\n\r\n      const parts = msg.content\r\n      const first = parts.findIndex((part) => part.type === \"tool-call\")\r\n      if (first === -1) return [msg]\r\n      if (!parts.slice(first).some((part) => part.type !== \"tool-call\")) return [msg]\r\n      return [\r\n        { ...msg, content: parts.filter((part) => part.type !== \"tool-call\") },\r\n        { ...msg, content: parts.filter((part) => part.type === \"tool-call\") },\r\n      ]\r\n    })\r\n  }\r\n  if (\r\n    model.providerID === \"mistral\" ||\r\n    model.api.id.toLowerCase().includes(\"mistral\") ||\r\n    model.api.id.toLocaleLowerCase().includes(\"devstral\")\r\n  ) {\r\n    const scrub = (id: string) => {\r\n      return id\r\n        .replace(/[^a-zA-Z0-9]/g, \"\") // Remove non-alphanumeric characters\r\n        .substring(0, 9) // Take first 9 characters\r\n        .padEnd(9, \"0\") // Pad with zeros if less than 9 characters\r\n    }\r\n    const result: ModelMessage[] = []\r\n    for (let i = 0; i < msgs.length; i++) {\r\n      const msg = msgs[i]\r\n      const nextMsg = msgs[i + 1]\r\n\r\n      if (msg.role === \"assistant\" && Array.isArray(msg.content)) {\r\n        msg.content = msg.content.map((part) => {\r\n          if (part.type === \"tool-call\" || part.type === \"tool-result\") {\r\n            return { ...part, toolCallId: scrub(part.toolCallId) }\r\n          }\r\n          return part\r\n        })\r\n      }\r\n      if (msg.role === \"tool\" && Array.isArray(msg.content)) {\r\n        msg.content = msg.content.map((part) => {\r\n          if (part.type === \"tool-result\") {\r\n            return { ...part, toolCallId: scrub(part.toolCallId) }\r\n          }\r\n          return part\r\n        })\r\n      }\r\n      result.push(msg)\r\n\r\n      // Fix message sequence: tool messages cannot be followed by user messages\r\n      if (msg.role === \"tool\" && nextMsg?.role === \"user\") {\r\n        result.push({\r\n          role: \"assistant\",\r\n          content: [\r\n            {\r\n              type: \"text\",\r\n              text: \"Done.\",\r\n            },\r\n          ],\r\n        })\r\n      }\r\n    }\r\n    return result\r\n  }\r\n\r\n  // Detect whether the model uses reasoning/thinking and determine the\r\n  // providerOptions key/field for reasoning_content. For models without\r\n  // interleaved configured (e.g., DeepSeek via @ai-sdk/openai-compatible),\r\n  // default to the OpenAI-compatible reasoning_content field.\r\n  const interleaved = model.capabilities.interleaved\r\n  const isInterleaved = typeof interleaved === \"object\" && interleaved.field\r\n  const field = isInterleaved ? interleaved.field : \"reasoning_content\"\r\n  const key = providerOptionsKey(model)\r\n\r\n  // Check if we need to handle reasoning parts:\r\n  // - interleaved explicitly configured, OR\r\n  // - model has reasoning capability, OR\r\n  // - messages already contain reasoning parts (from DB replay)\r\n  const hasReasoningContent =\r\n    isInterleaved ||\r\n    model.capabilities.reasoning ||\r\n    msgs.some((msg) =>\r\n      msg.role === \"assistant\" &&\r\n      Array.isArray(msg.content) &&\r\n      msg.content.some((part: any) => part.type === \"reasoning\"),\r\n    )\r\n\r\n  if (hasReasoningContent) {\r\n    // @ai-sdk/deepseek 原生处理 reasoning，不走 providerOptions 注入。\r\n    // convertToDeepSeekChatMessages() 直接从 content 中读取 reasoning part，\r\n    // 不要剥离，保留在 content 数组里。\r\n    if (model.api.npm === \"@ai-sdk/deepseek\") {\r\n      return msgs.map((msg) => ({\r\n        ...msg,\r\n        providerOptions: {\r\n          ...msg.providerOptions,\r\n          [key]: {\r\n            ...msg.providerOptions?.[key],\r\n            thinking: { type: \"enabled\" },\r\n          },\r\n        },\r\n      }))\r\n    }\r\n\r\n    return msgs.map((msg) => {\r\n      if (msg.role === \"assistant\" && Array.isArray(msg.content)) {\r\n        const reasoningParts = msg.content.filter((part: any) => part.type === \"reasoning\")\r\n        const reasoningText = reasoningParts.map((part: any) => part.text).join(\"\")\r\n\r\n        // Filter out reasoning parts from content\r\n        const filteredContent = msg.content.filter((part: any) => part.type !== \"reasoning\")\r\n\r\n        // DeepSeek reasoning API requires ALL assistant messages in the conversation\r\n        // history to carry reasoning_content (even empty string). Old DB-replayed\r\n        // messages may have no reasoning parts at all — inject empty string for those.\r\n        return {\r\n          ...msg,\r\n          content: filteredContent,\r\n          providerOptions: {\r\n            ...msg.providerOptions,\r\n            [key]: {\r\n              ...msg.providerOptions?.[key],\r\n              [field]: reasoningText || \"\",\r\n            },\r\n          },\r\n        }\r\n      }\r\n\r\n      // Also handle string-content assistant messages (old DB format).\r\n      // Inject empty reasoning_content to satisfy DeepSeek API requirement.\r\n      if (msg.role === \"assistant\" && typeof msg.content === \"string\") {\r\n        return {\r\n          ...msg,\r\n          providerOptions: {\r\n            ...msg.providerOptions,\r\n            [key]: {\r\n              ...msg.providerOptions?.[key],\r\n              [field]: \"\",\r\n            },\r\n          },\r\n        }\r\n      }\r\n\r\n      return msg\r\n    })\r\n  }\r\n\r\n  return msgs\r\n}\r\n\r\nfunction applyCaching(msgs: ModelMessage[], model: Provider.Model): ModelMessage[] {\r\n  const system = msgs.filter((msg) => msg.role === \"system\").slice(0, 2)\r\n  const final = msgs.filter((msg) => msg.role !== \"system\").slice(-2)\r\n\r\n  const key = providerOptionsKey(model)\r\n  const providerOptions = {\r\n    anthropic: {\r\n      cacheControl: { type: \"ephemeral\" },\r\n    },\r\n    openrouter: {\r\n      cacheControl: { type: \"ephemeral\" },\r\n    },\r\n    bedrock: {\r\n      cachePoint: { type: \"default\" },\r\n    },\r\n    [key]: {\r\n      cache_control: { type: \"ephemeral\" },\r\n    },\r\n    copilot: {\r\n      copilot_cache_control: { type: \"ephemeral\" },\r\n    },\r\n    alibaba: {\r\n      cacheControl: { type: \"ephemeral\" },\r\n    },\r\n  }\r\n\r\n  for (const msg of unique([...system, ...final])) {\r\n    const useMessageLevelOptions =\r\n      model.providerID === \"anthropic\" ||\r\n      model.providerID.includes(\"bedrock\") ||\r\n      model.api.npm === \"@ai-sdk/amazon-bedrock\"\r\n    const shouldUseContentOptions = !useMessageLevelOptions && Array.isArray(msg.content) && msg.content.length > 0\r\n\r\n    if (shouldUseContentOptions) {\r\n      const lastContent = msg.content[msg.content.length - 1]\r\n      if (\r\n        lastContent &&\r\n        typeof lastContent === \"object\" &&\r\n        lastContent.type !== \"tool-approval-request\" &&\r\n        lastContent.type !== \"tool-approval-response\"\r\n      ) {\r\n        lastContent.providerOptions = mergeDeep(lastContent.providerOptions ?? {}, providerOptions)\r\n        continue\r\n      }\r\n    }\r\n\r\n    msg.providerOptions = mergeDeep(msg.providerOptions ?? {}, providerOptions)\r\n  }\r\n\r\n  return msgs\r\n}\r\n\r\nfunction unsupportedParts(msgs: ModelMessage[], model: Provider.Model): ModelMessage[] {\r\n  return msgs.map((msg) => {\r\n    if (msg.role !== \"user\" || !Array.isArray(msg.content)) return msg\r\n\r\n    const filtered = msg.content.map((part) => {\r\n      if (part.type !== \"file\" && part.type !== \"image\") return part\r\n\r\n      // Check for empty base64 image data\r\n      if (part.type === \"image\") {\r\n        const imageStr = String(part.image)\r\n        if (imageStr.startsWith(\"data:\")) {\r\n          const match = imageStr.match(/^data:([^;]+);base64,(.*)$/)\r\n          if (match && (!match[2] || match[2].length === 0)) {\r\n            return {\r\n              type: \"text\" as const,\r\n              text: \"ERROR: Image file is empty or corrupted. Please provide a valid image.\",\r\n            }\r\n          }\r\n        }\r\n      }\r\n\r\n      const mime = part.type === \"image\" ? String(part.image).split(\";\")[0].replace(\"data:\", \"\") : part.mediaType\r\n      const filename = part.type === \"file\" ? part.filename : undefined\r\n      const modality = mimeToModality(mime)\r\n      if (!modality) return part\r\n      if (model.capabilities.input[modality]) return part\r\n\r\n      const name = filename ? `\"${filename}\"` : modality\r\n      return {\r\n        type: \"text\" as const,\r\n        text: `ERROR: Cannot read ${name} (this model does not support ${modality} input). Inform the user.`,\r\n      }\r\n    })\r\n\r\n    return { ...msg, content: filtered }\r\n  })\r\n}\r\n\r\nexport function message(msgs: ModelMessage[], model: Provider.Model, options: Record<string, unknown>) {\r\n  msgs = unsupportedParts(msgs, model)\r\n  msgs = normalizeMessages(msgs, model, options)\r\n  if (\r\n    (model.providerID === \"anthropic\" ||\r\n      model.providerID === \"google-vertex-anthropic\" ||\r\n      model.api.id.includes(\"anthropic\") ||\r\n      model.api.id.includes(\"claude\") ||\r\n      model.id.includes(\"anthropic\") ||\r\n      model.id.includes(\"claude\") ||\r\n      model.api.npm === \"@ai-sdk/anthropic\" ||\r\n      model.api.npm === \"@ai-sdk/alibaba\") &&\r\n    model.api.npm !== \"@ai-sdk/gateway\"\r\n  ) {\r\n    msgs = applyCaching(msgs, model)\r\n  }\r\n\r\n  // Remap providerOptions keys from stored providerID to expected SDK key\r\n  const key = sdkKey(model.api.npm)\r\n  if (key && key !== model.providerID) {\r\n    const remap = (opts: Record<string, any> | undefined) => {\r\n      if (!opts) return opts\r\n      if (!(model.providerID in opts)) return opts\r\n      const result = { ...opts }\r\n      result[key] = result[model.providerID]\r\n      delete result[model.providerID]\r\n      return result\r\n    }\r\n\r\n    msgs = msgs.map((msg) => {\r\n      if (!Array.isArray(msg.content)) return { ...msg, providerOptions: remap(msg.providerOptions) }\r\n      return {\r\n        ...msg,\r\n        providerOptions: remap(msg.providerOptions),\r\n        content: msg.content.map((part) => {\r\n          if (part.type === \"tool-approval-request\" || part.type === \"tool-approval-response\") {\r\n            return { ...part }\r\n          }\r\n          return { ...part, providerOptions: remap(part.providerOptions) }\r\n        }),\r\n      } as typeof msg\r\n    })\r\n  }\r\n\r\n  return msgs\r\n}\r\n\r\nexport function temperature(model: Provider.Model) {\r\n  const id = model.id.toLowerCase()\r\n  if (id.includes(\"qwen\")) return 0.55\r\n  if (id.includes(\"claude\")) return undefined\r\n  if (id.includes(\"gemini\")) return 1.0\r\n  if (id.includes(\"glm-4.6\")) return 1.0\r\n  if (id.includes(\"glm-4.7\")) return 1.0\r\n  if (id.includes(\"minimax-m2\")) return 1.0\r\n  if (id.includes(\"kimi-k2\")) {\r\n    // kimi-k2-thinking & kimi-k2.5 && kimi-k2p5 && kimi-k2-5\r\n    if ([\"thinking\", \"k2.\", \"k2p\", \"k2-5\"].some((s) => id.includes(s))) {\r\n      return 1.0\r\n    }\r\n    return 0.6\r\n  }\r\n  return undefined\r\n}\r\n\r\nexport function topP(model: Provider.Model) {\r\n  const id = model.id.toLowerCase()\r\n  if (id.includes(\"qwen\")) return 1\r\n  if ([\"minimax-m2\", \"gemini\", \"kimi-k2.5\", \"kimi-k2p5\", \"kimi-k2-5\"].some((s) => id.includes(s))) {\r\n    return 0.95\r\n  }\r\n  return undefined\r\n}\r\n\r\nexport function topK(model: Provider.Model) {\r\n  const id = model.id.toLowerCase()\r\n  if (id.includes(\"minimax-m2\")) {\r\n    if ([\"m2.\", \"m25\", \"m21\"].some((s) => id.includes(s))) return 40\r\n    return 20\r\n  }\r\n  if (id.includes(\"gemini\")) return 64\r\n  return undefined\r\n}\r\n\r\nconst WIDELY_SUPPORTED_EFFORTS = [\"low\", \"medium\", \"high\"]\r\nconst OPENAI_EFFORTS = [\"none\", \"minimal\", ...WIDELY_SUPPORTED_EFFORTS, \"xhigh\"]\r\n\r\nfunction anthropicAdaptiveEfforts(apiId: string): string[] | null {\r\n  if ([\"opus-4-7\", \"opus-4.7\"].some((v) => apiId.includes(v))) {\r\n    return [\"low\", \"medium\", \"high\", \"xhigh\", \"max\"]\r\n  }\r\n  if ([\"opus-4-6\", \"opus-4.6\", \"sonnet-4-6\", \"sonnet-4.6\"].some((v) => apiId.includes(v))) {\r\n    return [\"low\", \"medium\", \"high\", \"max\"]\r\n  }\r\n  return null\r\n}\r\n\r\nexport function variants(model: Provider.Model): Record<string, Record<string, any>> {\r\n  if (!model.capabilities.reasoning) return {}\r\n\r\n  const id = model.id.toLowerCase()\r\n  const adaptiveEfforts = anthropicAdaptiveEfforts(model.api.id)\r\n  if (\r\n    id.includes(\"deepseek\") ||\r\n    id.includes(\"minimax\") ||\r\n    id.includes(\"glm\") ||\r\n    id.includes(\"kimi\") ||\r\n    id.includes(\"k2p\") ||\r\n    id.includes(\"qwen\") ||\r\n    id.includes(\"big-pickle\")\r\n  )\r\n    return {}\r\n\r\n  // see: https://docs.x.ai/docs/guides/reasoning#control-how-hard-the-model-thinks\r\n  if (id.includes(\"grok\") && id.includes(\"grok-3-mini\")) {\r\n    if (model.api.npm === \"@openrouter/ai-sdk-provider\") {\r\n      return {\r\n        low: { reasoning: { effort: \"low\" } },\r\n        high: { reasoning: { effort: \"high\" } },\r\n      }\r\n    }\r\n    return {\r\n      low: { reasoningEffort: \"low\" },\r\n      high: { reasoningEffort: \"high\" },\r\n    }\r\n  }\r\n  if (id.includes(\"grok\")) return {}\r\n\r\n  switch (model.api.npm) {\r\n    case \"@openrouter/ai-sdk-provider\":\r\n      if (!model.id.includes(\"gpt\") && !model.id.includes(\"gemini-3\") && !model.id.includes(\"claude\")) return {}\r\n      return Object.fromEntries(OPENAI_EFFORTS.map((effort) => [effort, { reasoning: { effort } }]))\r\n\r\n    case \"@ai-sdk/gateway\":\r\n      if (model.id.includes(\"anthropic\")) {\r\n        if (adaptiveEfforts) {\r\n          return Object.fromEntries(\r\n            adaptiveEfforts.map((effort) => [\r\n              effort,\r\n              {\r\n                thinking: {\r\n                  type: \"adaptive\",\r\n                },\r\n                effort,\r\n              },\r\n            ]),\r\n          )\r\n        }\r\n        return {\r\n          high: {\r\n            thinking: {\r\n              type: \"enabled\",\r\n              budgetTokens: 16000,\r\n            },\r\n          },\r\n          max: {\r\n            thinking: {\r\n              type: \"enabled\",\r\n              budgetTokens: 31999,\r\n            },\r\n          },\r\n        }\r\n      }\r\n      if (model.id.includes(\"google\")) {\r\n        if (id.includes(\"2.5\")) {\r\n          return {\r\n            high: {\r\n              thinkingConfig: {\r\n                includeThoughts: true,\r\n                thinkingBudget: 16000,\r\n              },\r\n            },\r\n            max: {\r\n              thinkingConfig: {\r\n                includeThoughts: true,\r\n                thinkingBudget: 24576,\r\n              },\r\n            },\r\n          }\r\n        }\r\n        return Object.fromEntries(\r\n          [\"low\", \"high\"].map((effort) => [\r\n            effort,\r\n            {\r\n              includeThoughts: true,\r\n              thinkingLevel: effort,\r\n            },\r\n          ]),\r\n        )\r\n      }\r\n      return Object.fromEntries(OPENAI_EFFORTS.map((effort) => [effort, { reasoningEffort: effort }]))\r\n\r\n    case \"@ai-sdk/github-copilot\":\r\n      if (model.id.includes(\"gemini\")) {\r\n        // currently github copilot only returns thinking\r\n        return {}\r\n      }\r\n      if (model.id.includes(\"claude\")) {\r\n        return Object.fromEntries(WIDELY_SUPPORTED_EFFORTS.map((effort) => [effort, { reasoningEffort: effort }]))\r\n      }\r\n      const copilotEfforts = iife(() => {\r\n        if (id.includes(\"5.1-codex-max\") || id.includes(\"5.2\") || id.includes(\"5.3\"))\r\n          return [...WIDELY_SUPPORTED_EFFORTS, \"xhigh\"]\r\n        const arr = [...WIDELY_SUPPORTED_EFFORTS]\r\n        if (id.includes(\"gpt-5\") && model.release_date >= \"2025-12-04\") arr.push(\"xhigh\")\r\n        return arr\r\n      })\r\n      return Object.fromEntries(\r\n        copilotEfforts.map((effort) => [\r\n          effort,\r\n          {\r\n            reasoningEffort: effort,\r\n            reasoningSummary: \"auto\",\r\n            include: [\"reasoning.encrypted_content\"],\r\n          },\r\n        ]),\r\n      )\r\n\r\n    case \"@ai-sdk/cerebras\":\r\n    // https://v5.ai-sdk.dev/providers/ai-sdk-providers/cerebras\r\n    case \"@ai-sdk/togetherai\":\r\n    // https://v5.ai-sdk.dev/providers/ai-sdk-providers/togetherai\r\n    case \"@ai-sdk/xai\":\r\n    // https://v5.ai-sdk.dev/providers/ai-sdk-providers/xai\r\n    case \"@ai-sdk/deepinfra\":\r\n    // https://v5.ai-sdk.dev/providers/ai-sdk-providers/deepinfra\r\n    case \"venice-ai-sdk-provider\":\r\n    // https://docs.venice.ai/overview/guides/reasoning-models#reasoning-effort\r\n    case \"@ai-sdk/openai-compatible\":\r\n      return Object.fromEntries(WIDELY_SUPPORTED_EFFORTS.map((effort) => [effort, { reasoningEffort: effort }]))\r\n\r\n    case \"@ai-sdk/azure\":\r\n      // https://v5.ai-sdk.dev/providers/ai-sdk-providers/azure\r\n      if (id === \"o1-mini\") return {}\r\n      const azureEfforts = [\"low\", \"medium\", \"high\"]\r\n      if (id.includes(\"gpt-5-\") || id === \"gpt-5\") {\r\n        azureEfforts.unshift(\"minimal\")\r\n      }\r\n      return Object.fromEntries(\r\n        azureEfforts.map((effort) => [\r\n          effort,\r\n          {\r\n            reasoningEffort: effort,\r\n            reasoningSummary: \"auto\",\r\n            include: [\"reasoning.encrypted_content\"],\r\n          },\r\n        ]),\r\n      )\r\n    case \"@ai-sdk/openai\":\r\n      // https://v5.ai-sdk.dev/providers/ai-sdk-providers/openai\r\n      if (id === \"gpt-5-pro\") return {}\r\n      const openaiEfforts = iife(() => {\r\n        if (id.includes(\"codex\")) {\r\n          if (id.includes(\"5.2\") || id.includes(\"5.3\")) return [...WIDELY_SUPPORTED_EFFORTS, \"xhigh\"]\r\n          return WIDELY_SUPPORTED_EFFORTS\r\n        }\r\n        const arr = [...WIDELY_SUPPORTED_EFFORTS]\r\n        if (id.includes(\"gpt-5-\") || id === \"gpt-5\") {\r\n          arr.unshift(\"minimal\")\r\n        }\r\n        if (model.release_date >= \"2025-11-13\") {\r\n          arr.unshift(\"none\")\r\n        }\r\n        if (model.release_date >= \"2025-12-04\") {\r\n          arr.push(\"xhigh\")\r\n        }\r\n        return arr\r\n      })\r\n      return Object.fromEntries(\r\n        openaiEfforts.map((effort) => [\r\n          effort,\r\n          {\r\n            reasoningEffort: effort,\r\n            reasoningSummary: \"auto\",\r\n            include: [\"reasoning.encrypted_content\"],\r\n          },\r\n        ]),\r\n      )\r\n\r\n    case \"@ai-sdk/anthropic\":\r\n    // https://v5.ai-sdk.dev/providers/ai-sdk-providers/anthropic\r\n    case \"@ai-sdk/google-vertex/anthropic\":\r\n      // https://v5.ai-sdk.dev/providers/ai-sdk-providers/google-vertex#anthropic-provider\r\n\r\n      if (model.providerID === \"github-copilot\") {\r\n        if (model.api.id.includes(\"opus-4.7\")) {\r\n          return Object.fromEntries([\"medium\"].map((effort) => [effort, { reasoningEffort: effort }]))\r\n        }\r\n      }\r\n\r\n      if (adaptiveEfforts) {\r\n        return Object.fromEntries(\r\n          adaptiveEfforts.map((effort) => [\r\n            effort,\r\n            {\r\n              thinking: {\r\n                type: \"adaptive\",\r\n                ...(model.api.id.includes(\"opus-4-7\") || model.api.id.includes(\"opus-4.7\")\r\n                  ? { display: \"summarized\" }\r\n                  : {}),\r\n              },\r\n              effort,\r\n            },\r\n          ]),\r\n        )\r\n      }\r\n\r\n      return {\r\n        high: {\r\n          thinking: {\r\n            type: \"enabled\",\r\n            budgetTokens: Math.min(16_000, Math.floor(model.limit.output / 2 - 1)),\r\n          },\r\n        },\r\n        max: {\r\n          thinking: {\r\n            type: \"enabled\",\r\n            budgetTokens: Math.min(31_999, model.limit.output - 1),\r\n          },\r\n        },\r\n      }\r\n\r\n    case \"@ai-sdk/amazon-bedrock\":\r\n      // https://v5.ai-sdk.dev/providers/ai-sdk-providers/amazon-bedrock\r\n      if (adaptiveEfforts) {\r\n        return Object.fromEntries(\r\n          adaptiveEfforts.map((effort) => [\r\n            effort,\r\n            {\r\n              reasoningConfig: {\r\n                type: \"adaptive\",\r\n                maxReasoningEffort: effort,\r\n                ...(model.api.id.includes(\"opus-4-7\") || model.api.id.includes(\"opus-4.7\")\r\n                  ? { display: \"summarized\" }\r\n                  : {}),\r\n              },\r\n            },\r\n          ]),\r\n        )\r\n      }\r\n      // For Anthropic models on Bedrock, use reasoningConfig with budgetTokens\r\n      if (model.api.id.includes(\"anthropic\")) {\r\n        return {\r\n          high: {\r\n            reasoningConfig: {\r\n              type: \"enabled\",\r\n              budgetTokens: 16000,\r\n            },\r\n          },\r\n          max: {\r\n const rawSlug = i > 0 ? model.api.id.slice(0, i) : undefined\r\n    const slug = rawSlug ? 	{
		"content": "现在我已经完整阅读了所有相关的核心文件，下面是详细分析。\n\n---\n\n## opencode Provider 系统分析\n\n### 1. 整体架构概览\n\nProvider 系统是一个**分层加载、可插件扩展、基于 Effect 架构**的 AI 模型提供者管理系统。核心代码位于 `packages/opencode/src/provider/` 目录下：\n\n```\nprovider/\n├── index.ts          # 命名空间导出\n├── provider.ts       # 核心：Provider 服务层（加载、初始化、查询、获取 LanguageModel）\n├── schema.ts         # ProviderID / ModelID 的 branded types\n├── models.ts         # 从 models.dev 远程拉取/本地缓存的 provider & model 数据\n├── auth.ts           # Provider 认证（OAuth / API Key）\n├── error.ts          # API 调用错误的解析（上下文溢出、配额超限等）\n├── transform.ts      # 消息转换、推理变体、缓存注入等\n└── sdk/\n    └── copilot/      # GitHub Copilot 自定义 SDK（chat / responses）\n```\n\n### 2. 数据来源：三层模型发现\n\nProvider 系统从三个渠道获取 provider 和 model 信息，**层层覆盖**：\n\n#### 层 1: models.dev（远程 + 本地快照）\n- `models.ts` 中的 `Data` 是一个 lazy initializer\n- **加载顺序**：本地 cache 文件 → 构建时快照 `models-snapshot.js` → 远程 `https://models.dev/api.json`\n- 返回一个 `Record<string, Provider>`，每个 Provider 包含 `{ id, name, env, models[] }`\n- 后台每 60 分钟自动刷新\n\n#### 层 2: 配置文件（`opencode.json` 中的 `provider` 字段）\n- 用户可以通过配置文件自定义 provider\n- 可以**新增 provider**，也可以**覆盖已有的 models.dev provider**（覆盖 name、models、options 等）\n- 支持 `whitelist` / `blacklist` 筛选模型\n- 支持 `enabled_providers` / `disabled_providers` 全局开关\n\n#### 层 3: 环境变量 + 已存储的 API Key\n- 读取 `Env` 中的环境变量（每个 provider 的 `env` 字段定义了它监听的变量名）\n- 读取 `Auth` 中已存储的 API Key / OAuth token\n\n### 3. Provider 加载流程（`provider.ts` 中的 `layer`）\n\n核心初始化流程在 `layer`（一个 Effect Layer）中：\n\n```\n1. 读取 config     → 获取用户配置、enabled/disabled\n2. 加载 models.dev → 得到 database（基础模型数据）\n3. 加载 config providers → 覆盖/扩充 database\n4. 加载环境变量    → 检查 env 中是否有对应 provider 的 API key\n5. 加载 Auth API keys → 检查已存储的 auth 信息\n6. 加载插件 auth loader\n7. 执行 custom() 函数 → 为每个 provider 运行自定义初始化逻辑\n8. 重新应用 config → 确保用户配置覆盖生效\n9. 运行 discoverModels（如 GitLab 的动态模型发现）\n10. 运行插件 provider hooks\n11. 过滤：disabled、alpha/deprecated、whitelist/blacklist\n```\n\n关键函数 `custom(dep)` 为每个已知 provider 定义了**定制化初始化逻辑**，包括：\n- `autoload`: 是否自动加载（无需用户显式配置）\n- `getModel`: 自定义模型获取函数（如 `github-copilot` 判断用 `chat()` 还是 `responses()`）\n- `vars`: 环境变量映射（如 `google-vertex` 设置 `GOOGLE_VERTEX_PROJECT`）\n- `options`: 传递给 SDK 的默认选项（如 `anthropic` 注入 headers）\n- `discoverModels`: 动态模型发现（如 `gitlab` 从 GitLab API 获取 workflow models）\n\n### 4. 内置 Provider 列表\n\n系统通过 `BUNDLED_PROVIDERS`（静态导入映射）和 `custom()`（动态初始化逻辑）支持以下提供者：\n\n| npm 包 | 提供者 |\n|---|---|\n| `@ai-sdk/amazon-bedrock` | Amazon Bedrock |\n| `@ai-sdk/anthropic` | Anthropic (Claude) |\n| `@ai-sdk/azure` | Azure OpenAI |\n| `@ai-sdk/google` | Google Gemini |\n| `@ai-sdk/google-vertex` | Google Vertex AI |\n| `@ai-sdk/google-vertex/anthropic` | Vertex Anthropic |\n| `@ai-sdk/openai` | OpenAI |\n| `@ai-sdk/openai-compatible` | 通用 OpenAI 兼容 |\n| `@openrouter/ai-sdk-provider` | OpenRouter |\n| `@ai-sdk/xai` | xAI (Grok) |\n| `@ai-sdk/mistral` | Mistral |\n| `@ai-sdk/groq` | Groq |\n| `@ai-sdk/deepinfra` | DeepInfra |\n| `@ai-sdk/deepseek` | DeepSeek |\n| `@ai-sdk/cerebras` | Cerebras |\n| `@ai-sdk/cohere` | Cohere |\n| `@ai-sdk/gateway` | AI Gateway |\n| `@ai-sdk/togetherai` | Together AI |\n| `@ai-sdk/perplexity` | Perplexity |\n| `@ai-sdk/vercel` | Vercel |\n| `@ai-sdk/alibaba` | Alibaba |\n| `@ai-sdk/github-copilot` | GitHub Copilot (自定义 SDK) |\n| `gitlab-ai-provider` | GitLab Duo |\n| `venice-ai-sdk-provider` | Venice.ai |\n\n另外还有 `opencode`（自有推断服务）、`sap-ai-core`、`cloudflare-workers-ai`、`cloudflare-ai-gateway`、`llmgateway`、`nvidia`、`kilo`、`zenmux` 等。\n\n### 5. SDK 解析与模型实例化\n\n`resolveSDK()` 函数负责将 `Model` 解析为 AI SDK 的 `LanguageModelV3`：\n\n1. 从 provider options 和 model api 信息拼接 `baseURL`\n2. 注入 API key、headers\n3. 设置自定义 `fetch`（含超时、SSE chunk timeout、OpenAI itemId 清理）\n4. 先查 `BUNDLED_PROVIDERS`（已内联的 npm 包，无需额外安装）\n5. 否则通过 `Npm.add(npm_package)` 按需安装\n6. 动态 `import` 并调用 `createXxx()` 工厂函数\n7. 结果缓存到 `sdk Map`（以 `providerID + npm + options` 的 hash 为 key）\n\n`getLanguage()` 进一步将 SDK 实例与 model 绑定：\n- 如果该 provider 有自定义 `modelLoaders`（如 `github-copilot` 的 `chat()` vs `responses()` 切换），走自定义路径\n- 否则调用 `sdk.languageModel(model.api.id)`\n- 结果也缓存（key = `${providerID}/${model.id}`）\n\n### 6. 认证系统（`auth.ts`）\n\n`ProviderAuth` 服务提供：\n- `methods()`: 返回每个 provider 的认证方法（OAuth / API Key + 交互式 prompts）\n- `authorize()`: 触发 OAuth 流程或 API Key 的验证\n- `callback()`: 处理 OAuth 回调，将 token 或 API key 存入 `Auth` 服务\n\n认证由**插件系统**驱动——插件可以声明 `auth` hook，定义认证方法和 UI 提示。\n\n### 7. 消息转换与推理变体（`transform.ts`）\n\n`transform.ts` 负责在调用模型前对消息进行各种**规范化处理**：\n\n- **`normalizeMessages()`**: 按 provider 清理消息格式（如 Anthropic 拒绝空内容、Mistral 的 toolCallId 清洗、DeepSeek 注入 reasoning_content）\n- **`unsupportedParts()`**: 检查模型是否支持用户发送的多模态内容，不支持则替换为错误文本\n- **`applyCaching()`**: 为支持缓存的 provider（Anthropic、Bedrock、OpenRouter 等）注入缓存控制标记\n- **`variants()`**: 为支持推理（reasoning）的模型生成变体配置（如 reasoningEffort 的高低级别）\n- **`options()` / `smallOptions()`**: 根据模型和 provider 生成默认的调用选项\n\n### 8. 配置结构（`config/provider.ts`）\n\n用户可在 `opencode.json` 中配置：\n\n```json\n{\n  \"provider\": {\n    \"anthropic\": {\n      \"api\": \"https://api.anthropic.com\",\n      \"name\": \"My Anthropic\",\n      \"env\": [\"ANTHROPIC_API_KEY\"],\n      \"options\": { \"baseURL\": \"...\" },\n      \"models\": {\n        \"claude-sonnet-4\": {\n          \"cost\": { \"input\": 3, \"output\": 15 },\n          \"limit\": { \"context\": 200000, \"output\": 8192 }\n        }\n      }\n    }\n  },\n  \"disabled_providers\": [\"some-provider\"],\n  \"enabled_providers\": [\"openai\", \"anthropic\"],\n  \"model\": \"anthropic/claude-sonnet-4\",\n  \"small_model\": \"anthropic/claude-haiku-4-5\"\n}\n```\n\n### 9. Service 接口\n\nProvider 服务暴露的核心接口：\n\n```typescript\ninterface Interface {\n  readonly list: () => Effect.Effect<Record<ProviderID, Info>>\n  readonly getProvider: (providerID: ProviderID) => Effect.Effect<Info>\n  readonly getModel: (providerID: ProviderID, modelID: ModelID) => Effect.Effect<Model>\n  readonly getLanguage: (model: Model) => Effect.Effect<LanguageModelV3>\n  readonly closest: (providerID: ProviderID, query: string[]) => Effect.Effect<...>\n  readonly getSmallModel: (providerID: ProviderID) => Effect.Effect<Model | undefined>\n  readonly defaultModel: () => Effect.Effect<{ providerID: ProviderID; modelID: ModelID }>\n}\n```\n\n### 10. 错误处理（`error.ts`）\n\n- `parseAPICallError()`: 将 AI SDK 的 `APICallError` 解析为 `context_overflow` 或 `api_error`\n- 支持大量 provider 的溢出错误模式匹配（Anthropic、OpenAI、Google、Bedrock、Groq 等）\n- 特殊处理 OpenAI 的 404 retryable 行为\n\n---\n\n### 总结\n\nopencode 的 Provider 系统是一个**高度可扩展的分层架构**：\n\n1. **数据层**：远程模型目录 → 配置文件 → 环境变量/Auth，逐层覆盖\n2. **加载层**：内置 bundled providers + 按需 npm 安装 + 自定义 SDK\n3. **定制层**：每个 provider 有独立的初始化逻辑（autoload、getModel、vars、options）\n4. **转换层**：消息规范化、缓存注入、推理变体、多模态过滤\n5. **插件层**：插件可以通过 `auth` 和 `provider` hooks 扩展认证方式和模型发现\n6. **认证层**：支持 OAuth 和 API Key 两种方式，由插件驱动交互流程",
		"reasoning_content": "现在我对 opencode 的 Provider 系统有了全面的了解。让我整理一下分析结果。",
		"role": "assistant"
	}
]
```

Model, s: State, envs: Record<string, string | undefined>) {\r\n      try {\r\n        using _ = log.time(\"getSDK\", {\r\n          providerID: model.providerID,\r\n        })\r\n        const options[\"baseURL\"] === \"string\" && options[\"baseURL\"] !== \"\" ? options[\"baseURL\"] : model.api.url\r\n          if (!url) return\r\n\r\n          const loader = \"${\" + key + \"}\"\r\n              url = url.replaceAll(field, value)\r\n            }\r\n          }\r\n\r\n          url = url.replace(/\\$\\{([^}]+)\\}/g, (item, key) => {\r\n            const
