         ...model.headers,\r\n          }\r\n\r\n        const key = Hash.fast(\r\n          JSON.stringify({\r\n            providerID: model.providerID,\r\n            npm: model.api.npm,\r\n            options,\r\n          }),\r\n        )\r\n        const existing = s.sdk.get(key)\r\n        if (existing) return existing\r\n\r\n        const customFetch = options[\"fetch\"]\r\n        const = customFetch ?? fetch\r\n          const opts = init ?? {}\r\n          const chunkAbortCtl = typeof chunkTimeout === \"number\" && chunkTimeout > 0 ? new AbortController() : undefined\r\n          const signals: AbortSignal[] = []\r\n\r\n          if (opts.signal) signals.push(opts.signal)\r\n          if (chunkAbortCtl) signals.push(chunkAbortCtl.signal)\r\n          if (options[\"timeout\"] signals.length === 0 ? null : signals.length === 1 ? signals[0] : AbortSignal.any(signals)\r\n          if (combined) opts.signal = combined\r\n\r\n          // Strip openai itemId metadata following what codex does\r\n          if (model.api.npm === \"@ai-sdk/openai\" && opts.body && opts.method === \"POST\") {\r\n            const body = JSON.parse(opts.body as string)\r\n            const item of body.input) {\r\n                if (\"id\" in item) {\r\n                  delete item.id\r\n                }\r\n              }\r\n              opts.body = JSON.stringify(body)\r\n            }\r\n          }\r\n\r\n          const res = await fetchFn(input, {\r\n            ...opts,\r\n            // @ts-ignore see here: https://github.com/oven-sh/bun/issues/16682\r\n            timeout: false,\r\n          })\r\n\r\n          if (!chunkAbortCtl) return res\r\n          return wrapSSE(res, chunkTimeout, chunkAbortCtl)\r\n        }\r\n\r\n        const bundledLoader =          })\r\n          const factory = await bundledLoader()\r\n          const loaded = factory({\r\n            name: model.providerID,\r\n            ...options,\r\n          })\r\n     log.info(\"loading local provider\", { pkg: model.api.npm })\r\n          installedPath = model.api.npm\r\n        }\r\n\r\n        // `installedPath` is a local entry path or an existing Effect.fn(\"Provider.defaultModel\")(function* () {\r\n      const cfg = yield* config.get()\r\n      if (cfg.model) return parseModel(cfg.model)\r\n\r\n      const s = yield* 			"content": "import { APICallError } from \"ai\"\r\nimport { STATUS_CODES } from \"http\"\r\nimport { iife } from \"@/util/iife\"\r\nimport type { ProviderID } from \"./schema\"\r\n\r\n// Adapted from overflow detection patterns in:\r\n// https://github.com/badlogic/pi-mono/blob/main/packages/ai/src/utils/overflow.ts\r\nconst OVERFLOW_PATTERNS = [\r\n  /prompt is too long/i, // Anthropic\r\n  /input is too long for requested model/i, // Amazon Bedrock\r\n  /exceeds the context window/i, // OpenAI (Completions + Responses API message text)\r\n  /input token count.*exceeds the maximum/i, // Google (Gemini)\r\n  /maximum prompt length is \\d+/i, // xAI (Grok)\r\n  /reduce the length of the messages/i, // Groq\r\n  /maximum context length is \\d+ tokens/i, // OpenRouter, DeepSeek, vLLM\r\n  /exceeds the limit of \\d+/i, // GitHub Copilot\r\n  /exceeds the available context size/i, // llama.cpp server\r\n  /greater than the context length/i, // LM Studio\r\n  /context window exceeds limit/i, // MiniMax\r\n  /exceeded model token limit/i, // Kimi For Coding, Moonshot\r\n  /context[_ ]length[_ ]exceeded/i, // Generic fallback\r\n  /request entity too large/i, // HTTP 413\r\n  /context length is only \\d+ tokens/i, // vLLM\r\n  /input length.*exceeds.*context length/i, // vLLM\r\n  /prompt too long; exceeded (?:max )?context length/i, // Ollama explicit overflow error\r\n  /too large for model with \\d+ maximum context length/i, // Mistral\r\n  /model_context_window_exceeded/i, // z.ai non-standard finish_reason surfaced as error text\r\n]\r\n\r\nfunction isOpenAiErrorRetryable(e: APICallError) {\r\n  const status = e.statusCode\r\n  if (!status) return e.isRetryable\r\n  // openai sometimes returns 404 for models that are actually available\r\n  return status === 404 || e.isRetryable\r\n}\r\n\r\n// Providers not reliably handled in this function:\r\n// - z.ai: can accept overflow silently (needs token-count/context-window checks)\r\nfunction isOverflow(message: string) {\r\n  if (OVERFLOW_PATTERNS.some((p) => p.test(message))) return true\r\n\r\n  // Providers/status patterns handled outside of regex list:\r\n  // - Cerebras: often returns \"400 (no body)\" / \"413 (no body)\"\r\n  // - Mistral: often returns \"400 (no body)\" / \"413 (no body)\"\r\n  return /^4(00|13)\\s*(status code)?\\s*\\(no body\\)/i.test(message)\r\n}\r\n\r\nfunction message(providerID: ProviderID, e: APICallError) {\r\n  return iife(() => {\r\n    const msg = e.message\r\n    if (msg === \"\") {\r\n      if (e.responseBody) return e.responseBody\r\n      if (e.statusCode) {\r\n        const err = STATUS_CODES[e.statusCode]\r\n        if (err) return err\r\n      }\r\n      return \"Unknown error\"\r\n    }\r\n\r\n    if (!e.responseBody || (e.statusCode && msg !== STATUS_CODES[e.statusCode])) {\r\n      return msg\r\n    }\r\n\r\n    try {\r\n      const body = JSON.parse(e.responseBody)\r\n      // try to extract common error message fields\r\n      const errMsg = body.message || body.error || body.error?.message\r\n      if (errMsg && typeof errMsg === \"string\") {\r\n        return `${msg}: ${errMsg}`\r\n      }\r\n    } catch {}\r\n\r\n    // If responseBody is HTML (e.g. from a gateway or proxy error page),\r\n    // provide a human-readable message instead of dumping raw markup\r\n    if (/^\\s*<!doctype|^\\s*<html/i.test(e.responseBody)) {\r\n      if (e.statusCode === 401) {\r\n        return \"Unauthorized: request was blocked by a gateway or proxy. Your authentication token may be missing or expired — try running `opencode auth login <your provider URL>` to re-authenticate.\"\r\n      }\r\n      if (e.statusCode === 403) {\r\n        return \"Forbidden: request was blocked by a gateway or proxy. You may not have permission to access this resource — check your account and provider settings.\"\r\n      }\r\n      return msg\r\n    }\r\n\r\n    return `${msg}: ${e.responseBody}`\r\n  }).trim()\r\n}\r\n\r\nfunction json(input: unknown) {\r\n  if (typeof input === \"string\") {\r\n    try {\r\n      const result = JSON.parse(input)\r\n      if (result && typeof result === \"object\") return result\r\n      return undefined\r\n    } catch {\r\n      return undefined\r\n    }\r\n  }\r\n  if (typeof input === \"object\" && input !== null) {\r\n    return input\r\n  }\r\n  return undefined\r\n}\r\n\r\nexport type ParsedStreamError =\r\n  | {\r\n      type: \"context_overflow\"\r\n      message: string\r\n      responseBody: string\r\n    }\r\n  | {\r\n      type: \"api_error\"\r\n      message: string\r\n      isRetryable: false\r\n      responseBody: string\r\n    }\r\n\r\nexport function parseStreamError(input: unknown): ParsedStreamError | undefined {\r\n  const body = json(input)\r\n  if (!body) return\r\n\r\n  const responseBody = JSON.stringify(body)\r\n  if (body.type !== \"error\") return\r\n\r\n  switch (body?.error?.code) {\r\n    case \"context_length_exceeded\":\r\n      return {\r\n        type: \"context_overflow\",\r\n        message: \"Input exceeds context window of this model\",\r\n        responseBody,\r\n      }\r\n    case \"insufficient_quota\":\r\n      return {\r\n        type: \"api_error\",\r\n        message: \"Quota exceeded.   })\r\n  }\r\n  if ([\"@ai-sdk/anthropic\", \"@ai-sdk/google-vertex/anthropic\"].includes(model.api.npm)) {\r\n    // Anthropic rejects assistant turns where tool_use blocks are followed by msgs = applyCaching(msgs, model)\r\n  }\r\n\r\n  // Remap providerOptions keys from stored providerID to expected SDK key\r\n  const key = sdkKey(model.api.npm)\r\n  if (key && key !== ...opts }\r\n      result[key] = result[model.providerID]\r\n      delete result[model.providerID]\r\n      return result\r\n    }\r\n\r\n    msgs = msgs.map((msg) => {\r\n      if content: msg.content.map((part) => {\r\n          if (part.type === \"tool-approval-request\" || part.type === \"tool-approval-response\") {\r\n            return { ...part }\r\n          }\r\n          return { ...part, providerOptions: remap(part.providerOptions) }\r\n        }),\r\n      } as typeof msg\r\n    })\r\n  }\r\n\r\n  return msgs\r\n}\r\n\r\nexport function temperature(model: Provider.Model) {\r\n  const id = model.id.toLowerCase()\r\n  if (id.includes(\"qwen\")) return 0.55\r\n  if (id.includes(\"claude\")) return undefined\r\n  if (id.includes(\"gemini\")) return 1.0\r\n undefined\r\n}\r\n\r\nexport function topP(model: Provider.Model) {\r\n  const id = model.id.toLowerCase()\r\n  if (id.includes(\"qwen\")) return 1\r\n  if ([\"minimax-m2\", \"gemini\", \"kimi-k2.5\", \"xhigh\"]\r\n\r\nfunction anthropicAdaptiveEfforts(apiId: string): string[] | null {\r\n  if ([\"opus-4-7\", \"opus-4.7\"].some((v) => apiId.includes(v))) {\r\n    return [\"low\", \"medium\", \"high\", \"xhigh\", \"max\"]\r\n  }\r\n  if ([\"opus-4-6\", \"opus-4.6\", \"sonnet-4-6\", \"sonnet-4.6\"].some((v) => apiId.includes(v))) {\r\n    return [\"low\", \"medium\", \"high\", \"max\"]\r\n  }\r\n  return null\r\n}\r\n\r\nexport function variants(model: Provider.Model): Record<string, Record<string, any>> {\r\n  if (!model.capabilities.reasoning) return {}\r\n\r\n  const id = input.model.api.id.includes(\"gpt-5.\") &&\r\n      !input.model.api.id.includes(\"codex\") &&\r\n      !input.model.api.id.includes(\"-chat\") &&\r\n      input.model.providerID !== \"azure\"\r\n === \"@ai-sdk/gateway\") {\r\n    result[\"gateway\"] = {\r\n      caching: \"auto\",\r\n    }\r\n  }\r\n\r\n  return result\r\n}\r\n\r\nexport function smallOptions(model: Provider.Model) {\r\n  if (\r\n    model.providerID === \"openai\" ||\r\n    model.api.npm === \"@ai-sdk/openai\" ||\r\n    model.api.npm === \"@ai-sdk/github-copilot\"\r\n  ) {\r\n    if (model.api.id.includes(\"gpt-5\")) reasoningEffort: \"minimal\" }\r\n    }\r\n    return { store: false }\r\n  }\r\n  if (model.providerID === \"google\") {\r\n    // gemini-3 uses thinkingLevel, gemini-2.5 uses thinkingBudget\r\n    if (model.api.id.includes(\"gemini-3\")) {\r\n      return { thinkingConfig: { thinkingLevel: \"minimal\" } }\r\n    }\r\n    return { thinkingConfig: { thinkingBudget: 0 } }\r\n  }\r\n  if (model.providerID === \"openrouter\" || model.providerID === \"llmgateway\") {\r\n    if (model.api.id.includes(\"google\")) {\r\n      return { reasoning: { enabled: false } }\r\n    }\r\n    return model ID prefix to provider slug used in providerOptions.\r\n// Example: \"amazon/nova-2-lite\" → \"bedrock\"\r\nconst SLUG_OVERRIDES: Record<string, string> = {\r\n  amazon: \"bedrock\",\r\n}\r\n\r\nexport function providerOptions(model: Provider.Model, options: { [x: string]: any }) {\r\n  if (model.api.npm === \"@ai-sdk/gateway\") {\r\n    // Gateway providerOptions are split across two namespaces:\r\n    // - `gateway`: gateway-native routing/caching controls (order, only, byok, etc.)\r\n    // - `<upstream slug>`: provider-specific model options (anthropic/openai/...)\r\n    // We keep `gateway` as-is and route every other top-level option under the\r\n    // model-derived upstream slug.\r\n    const i = model.api.id.indexOf(\"/\")\r\n    const rawSlug = i > 0 ? model.api.id.slice(0, i) : undefined\r\n    const slug = rawSlug ? (SLUG_OVERRIDES[rawSlug] ?? rawSlug) : undefined\r\n    const gateway = options.gateway\r\n    const rest = Object.fromEntries(Object.entries(options).filter(([k]) => k !== \"gateway\"))\r\n    const has = Object.keys(rest).length > 0\r\n\r\n    const result: Record<string, any> = {}\r\n    if (gateway !== undefined) result.gateway = gateway\r\n\r\n    if (has) {\r\n      if (slug) {\r\n        // Route model-specific options under the provider slug\r\n        result[slug] = rest\r\n      } else if (gateway && typeof gateway === \"object\" && !Array.isArray(gateway)) {\r\n        result.gateway = { ...gateway, ...rest }\r\n      } else {\r\n        result.gateway = rest\r\n      }\r\n    }\r\n\r\n    return result\r\n  }\r\n\r\n  const key = sdkKey(model.api.npm) ?? model.providerID\r\n  // @ai-sdk/azure delegates to OpenAIChatLanguageModel which reads from\r\n  // providerOptions[\"openai\"], but OpenAIResponsesLanguageModel checks\r\n  // \"azure\" first. Pass both so model options work on either code path.\r\n  if (model.api.npm === \"@ai-sdk/azure\") {\r\n    return { openai: options, azure: options }\r\n  }\r\n  return { [key]: options }\r\n}\r\n\r\nexport function maxOutputTokens(model: Provider.Model): number {\r\n  return Math.min(model.limit.output, OUTPUT_TOKEN_MAX) || OUTPUT_TOKEN_MAX\r\n}\r\n\r\nexport function schema(model: =>\r\n      typeof node === \"object\" && node !== null && !Array.isArray(node)\r\n    const hasCombiner = (node: unknown) =>\r\n      isPlainObject(node) && (Array.isArray(node.anyOf) || Array.isArray(node.oneOf) || Array.isArray(node.allOf))\r\n    const hasSchemaIntent = (node: unknown) => {\r\n      if (!isPlainObject(node)) return false\r\n      if (hasCombiner(node)) return true\r\n      return [\r\n        \"type\",\r\n        \"properties\",\r\n        \"items\",\r\n        \"prefixItems\",\r\n        \"enum\",\r\n        \"const\",\r\n        \"$ref\",\r\n        \"additionalProperties\",\r\n        \"patternProperties\",\r\n        \"required\",\r\n        \"not\",\r\n        \"if\",\r\n        \"then\",\r\n        \"else\",\r\n      ].some((key) => key in node)\r\n    }\r\n\r\n    const sanitizeGemini = (obj: any): any => {\r\n      if (obj === null || typeof obj !== \"object\") {\r\n        return obj\r\n      }\r\n\r\n      if (Array.isArray(obj)) {\r\n        return obj.map(sanitizeGemini)\r\n      }\r\n\r\n      const result: any = {}\r\n      for (const [key, value] of Object.entries(obj)) {\r\n        if (key === \"enum\" && Array.isArray(value)) {\r\n          // Convert all enum values to strings\r\n          result[key] = value.map((v) => String(v))\r\n          // If we have integer type with enum, change type to string\r\n          if (result.type === \"integer\" || result.type === \"number\") {\r\n            result.type = \"string\"\r\n          }\r\n        } else if (typeof value === \"object\" && value that exist in properties\r\n      if (result.type === \"object\" && result.properties && Array.isArray(result.required)) {\r\n        result.required = result.required.filter((field: any) => field in result.properties)\r\n      }\r\n\r\n      if (result.type === \"array\" && !hasCombiner(result)) {\r\n        if (result.items == null) {\r\n          result.items = {}\r\n        }\r\n        // result.properties\r\n        delete result.required\r\n      }\r\n\r\n      return result\r\n    }\r\n\r\n    schema = sanitizeGemini(schema)\r\n  }\r\n\r\n  return schema as JSONSchema7\r\n}\r\n",

## response

```json
{
	"choices": [
		{
			"index": 0,
			"message": {
				"content": "现在我已经完整阅读了所有相关的核心文件，下面是详细分析。\n\n---\n\n## opencode Provider 系统分析\n\n### 1. 整体架构概览\n\nProvider 系统是一个**分层加载、可插件扩展、基于 Effect 架构**的 AI 模型提供者管理系统。核心代码位于 `packages/opencode/src/provider/` 目录下：\n\n```\nprovider/\n├── index.ts          # 命名空间导出\n├── provider.ts       # 核心：Provider 服务层（加载、初始化、查询、获取 LanguageModel）\n├── schema.ts         # ProviderID / ModelID 的 branded types\n├── models.ts         # 从 models.dev 远程拉取/本地缓存的 provider & model 数据\n├── auth.ts           # Provider 认证（OAuth / API Key）\n├── error.ts          # API 调用错误的解析（上下文溢出、配额超限等）\n├── transform.ts      # 消息转换、推理变体、缓存注入等\n└── sdk/\n    └── copilot/      # GitHub Copilot 自定义 SDK（chat / responses）\n```\n\n### 2. 数据来源：三层模型发现\n\nProvider 系统从三个渠道获取 provider 和 model 信息，**层层覆盖**：\n\n#### 层 1: models.dev（远程 + 本地快照）\n- `models.ts` 中的 `Data` 是一个 lazy initializer\n- **加载顺序**：本地 cache 文件 → 构建时快照 `models-snapshot.js` → 远程 `https://models.dev/api.json`\n- 返回一个 `Record<string, Provider>`，每个 Provider 包含 `{ id, name, env, models[] }`\n- 后台每 60 分钟自动刷新\n\n#### 层 2: 配置文件（`opencode.json` 中的 `provider` 字段）\n- 用户可以通过配置文件自定义 provider\n- 可以**新增 provider**，也可以**覆盖已有的 models.dev provider**（覆盖 name、models、options 等）\n- 支持 `whitelist` / `blacklist` 筛选模型\n- 支持 `enabled_providers` / `disabled_providers` 全局开关\n\n#### 层 3: 环境变量 + 已存储的 API Key\n- 读取 `Env` 中的环境变量（每个 provider 的 `env` 字段定义了它监听的变量名）\n- 读取 `Auth` 中已存储的 API Key / OAuth token\n\n### 3. Provider 加载流程（`provider.ts` 中的 `layer`）\n\n核心初始化流程在 `layer`（一个 Effect Layer）中：\n\n```\n1. 读取 config     → 获取用户配置、enabled/disabled\n2. 加载 models.dev → 得到 database（基础模型数据）\n3. 加载 config providers → 覆盖/扩充 database\n4. 加载环境变量    → 检查 env 中是否有对应 provider 的 API key\n5. 加载 Auth API keys → 检查已存储的 auth 信息\n6. 加载插件 auth loader\n7. 执行 custom() 函数 → 为每个 provider 运行自定义初始化逻辑\n8. 重新应用 config → 确保用户配置覆盖生效\n9. 运行 discoverModels（如 GitLab 的动态模型发现）\n10. 运行插件 provider hooks\n11. 过滤：disabled、alpha/deprecated、whitelist/blacklist\n```\n\n关键函数 `custom(dep)` 为每个已知 provider 定义了**定制化初始化逻辑**，包括：\n- `autoload`: 是否自动加载（无需用户显式配置）\n- `getModel`: 自定义模型获取函数（如 `github-copilot` 判断用 `chat()` 还是 `responses()`）\n- `vars`: 环境变量映射（如 `google-vertex` 设置 `GOOGLE_VERTEX_PROJECT`）\n- `options`: 传递给 SDK 的默认选项（如 `anthropic` 注入 headers）\n- `discoverModels`: 动态模型发现（如 `gitlab` 从 GitLab API 获取 workflow models）\n\n### 4. 内置 Provider 列表\n\n系统通过 `BUNDLED_PROVIDERS`（静态导入映射）和 `custom()`（动态初始化逻辑）支持以下提供者：\n\n| npm 包 | 提供者 |\n|---|---|\n| `@ai-sdk/amazon-bedrock` | Amazon Bedrock |\n| `@ai-sdk/anthropic` | Anthropic (Claude) |\n| `@ai-sdk/azure` | Azure OpenAI |\n| `@ai-sdk/google` | Google Gemini |\n| `@ai-sdk/google-vertex` | Google Vertex AI |\n| `@ai-sdk/google-vertex/anthropic` | Vertex Anthropic |\n| `@ai-sdk/openai` | OpenAI |\n| `@ai-sdk/openai-compatible` | 通用 OpenAI 兼容 |\n| `@openrouter/ai-sdk-provider` | OpenRouter |\n| `@ai-sdk/xai` | xAI (Grok) |\n| `@ai-sdk/mistral` | Mistral |\n| `@ai-sdk/groq` | Groq |\n| `@ai-sdk/deepinfra` | DeepInfra |\n| `@ai-sdk/deepseek` | DeepSeek |\n| `@ai-sdk/cerebras` | Cerebras |\n| `@ai-sdk/cohere` | Cohere |\n| `@ai-sdk/gateway` | AI Gateway |\n| `@ai-sdk/togetherai` | Together AI |\n| `@ai-sdk/perplexity` | Perplexity |\n| `@ai-sdk/vercel` | Vercel |\n| `@ai-sdk/alibaba` | Alibaba |\n| `@ai-sdk/github-copilot` | GitHub Copilot (自定义 SDK) |\n| `gitlab-ai-provider` | GitLab Duo |\n| `venice-ai-sdk-provider` | Venice.ai |\n\n另外还有 `opencode`（自有推断服务）、`sap-ai-core`、`cloudflare-workers-ai`、`cloudflare-ai-gateway`、`llmgateway`、`nvidia`、`kilo`、`zenmux` 等。\n\n### 5. SDK 解析与模型实例化\n\n`resolveSDK()` 函数负责将 `Model` 解析为 AI SDK 的 `LanguageModelV3`：\n\n1. 从 provider options 和 model api 信息拼接 `baseURL`\n2. 注入 API key、headers\n3. 设置自定义 `fetch`（含超时、SSE chunk timeout、OpenAI itemId 清理）\n4. 先查 `BUNDLED_PROVIDERS`（已内联的 npm 包，无需额外安装）\n5. 否则通过 `Npm.add(npm_package)` 按需安装\n6. 动态 `import` 并调用 `createXxx()` 工厂函数\n7. 结果缓存到 `sdk Map`（以 `providerID + npm + options` 的 hash 为 key）\n\n`getLanguage()` 进一步将 SDK 实例与 model 绑定：\n- 如果该 provider 有自定义 `modelLoaders`（如 `github-copilot` 的 `chat()` vs `responses()` 切换），走自定义路径\n- 否则调用 `sdk.languageModel(model.api.id)`\n- 结果也缓存（key = `${providerID}/${model.id}`）\n\n### 6. 认证系统（`auth.ts`）\n\n`ProviderAuth` 服务提供：\n- `methods()`: 返回每个 provider 的认证方法（OAuth / API Key + 交互式 prompts）\n- `authorize()`: 触发 OAuth 流程或 API Key 的验证\n- `callback()`: 处理 OAuth 回调，将 token 或 API key 存入 `Auth` 服务\n\n认证由**插件系统**驱动——插件可以声明 `auth` hook，定义认证方法和 UI 提示。\n\n### 7. 消息转换与推理变体（`transform.ts`）\n\n`transform.ts` 负责在调用模型前对消息进行各种**规范化处理**：\n\n- **`normalizeMessages()`**: 按 provider 清理消息格式（如 Anthropic 拒绝空内容、Mistral 的 toolCallId 清洗、DeepSeek 注入 reasoning_content）\n- **`unsupportedParts()`**: 检查模型是否支持用户发送的多模态内容，不支持则替换为错误文本\n- **`applyCaching()`**: 为支持缓存的 provider（Anthropic、Bedrock、OpenRouter 等）注入缓存控制标记\n- **`variants()`**: 为支持推理（reasoning）的模型生成变体配置（如 reasoningEffort 的高低级别）\n- **`options()` / `smallOptions()`**: 根据模型和 provider 生成默认的调用选项\n\n### 8. 配置结构（`config/provider.ts`）\n\n用户可在 `opencode.json` 中配置：\n\n```json\n{\n  \"provider\": {\n    \"anthropic\": {\n      \"api\": \"https://api.anthropic.com\",\n      \"name\": \"My Anthropic\",\n      \"env\": [\"ANTHROPIC_API_KEY\"],\n      \"options\": { \"baseURL\": \"...\" },\n      \"models\": {\n        \"claude-sonnet-4\": {\n          \"cost\": { \"input\": 3, \"output\": 15 },\n          \"limit\": { \"context\": 200000, \"output\": 8192 }\n        }\n      }\n    }\n  },\n  \"disabled_providers\": [\"some-provider\"],\n  \"enabled_providers\": [\"openai\", \"anthropic\"],\n  \"model\": \"anthropic/claude-sonnet-4\",\n  \"small_model\": \"anthropic/claude-haiku-4-5\"\n}\n```\n\n### 9. Service 接口\n\nProvider 服务暴露的核心接口：\n\n```typescript\ninterface Interface {\n  readonly list: () => Effect.Effect<Record<ProviderID, Info>>\n  readonly getProvider: (providerID: ProviderID) => Effect.Effect<Info>\n  readonly getModel: (providerID: ProviderID, modelID: ModelID) => Effect.Effect<Model>\n  readonly getLanguage: (model: Model) => Effect.Effect<LanguageModelV3>\n  readonly closest: (providerID: ProviderID, query: string[]) => Effect.Effect<...>\n  readonly getSmallModel: (providerID: ProviderID) => Effect.Effect<Model | undefined>\n  readonly defaultModel: () => Effect.Effect<{ providerID: ProviderID; modelID: ModelID }>\n}\n```\n\n### 10. 错误处理（`error.ts`）\n\n- `parseAPICallError()`: 将 AI SDK 的 `APICallError` 解析为 `context_overflow` 或 `api_error`\n- 支持大量 provider 的溢出错误模式匹配（Anthropic、OpenAI、Google、Bedrock、Groq 等）\n- 特殊处理 OpenAI 的 404 retryable 行为\n\n---\n\n### 总结\n\nopencode 的 Provider 系统是一个**高度可扩展的分层架构**：\n\n1. **数据层**：远程模型目录 → 配置文件 → 环境变量/Auth，逐层覆盖\n2. **加载层**：内置 bundled providers + 按需 npm 安装 + 自定义 SDK\n3. **定制层**：每个 provider 有独立的初始化逻辑（autoload、getModel、vars、options）\n4. **转换层**：消息规范化、缓存注入、推理变体、多模态过滤\n5. **插件层**：插件可以通过 `auth` 和 `provider` hooks 扩展认证方式和模型发现\n6. **认证层**：支持 OAuth 和 API Key 两种方式，由插件驱动交互流程",
				"reasoning_content": "现在我对 opencode 的 Provider 系统有了全面的了解。让我整理一下分析结果。",
				"role": "assistant"
			}
		}
	]
}
```
